  Ahna  

1)  
The Path of Purpose  
There is no one in this world who lives without purpose. People live their social lives centered around their own purposes. The humanity that exists in the world today establishes purposes related to their businesses, studies, or professional fields and strives toward those goals.  
What the Good Requires  
So, what is the foundation upon which this purpose is built? Of course, it is centered around people, but it is about moving forward with that heart. The heart in this context always wishes for things to go well and not to go wrong. Whether it is flat or three-dimensional, whether it is contemporary or historical, it always hopes for things to go better. Therefore, the ultimate goal that purpose aims for is to reach a standard that all people like.  
The conscience of a person, needless to say, always follows the good. This good becomes the factor that enables humans to achieve something greater. Therefore, humans must establish their purposes according to the good. Regardless of their research fields, business areas, or any other fields, they must establish their purposes based on the good.  
Now, what content does the good itself possess? When analyzing whether the good is passive or active, the good itself does not wish to be passive. It always desires proactivity. Therefore, in any society or organization, the larger the organization, the more it seeks to move that society or organization to be subordinate to the realm of good standards.  
Why do people seek true goodness? It is because the good itself is not passive but active, and it does not bring injustice and loss to our lives but always brings benefits.  
For this reason, a person with a conscience is compelled to have their subjectivity based on the good. The reason they dislike being dominated by others lies there. Furthermore, the standard of the good that they desire based on their conscience does not seek limitations. Therefore, even if they are Korean, they do not wish to be only Korean. They desire to become global citizens even if they are Korean. If there is something higher, the good demands that they become that existence.  
Thus, humans must live a truly conscientious life. Those with true conscience must uphold the highest ideals centered on their subjectivity. The more conscientious a person is, the more they demand their absolute subjectivity and the absolute highest.  
What is connected to the direction in which purpose aims? Inevitably, ideals or higher aspirations are connected there. Therefore, purpose moves toward the realm of ideals. Then, what is that ideal? It is not something that moves within the realm of any people's thoughts, nor is it something that establishes its goals within any era. It seeks to find standards that transcend the temporality and historicity and go beyond regional limitations.  
Thus, the heart demands some relative ideal realm. When this standard becomes infinite, it demands an infinite environmental realm, and the subjectivity of the heart that demands that infinite relative ideal realm is also infinite, and therefore it demands the infinitely supreme. Because humans possess such a heart, we can conclude that they are noble.  
The path of purpose is the path toward ideals. Many people who have gone through the historical process lived according to their own whims, but purpose has pursued a higher good and more valuable things. It has sought a higher ideal.  
As history flows, as eras change, or as national sovereignty shifts, even if the environment changes in various ways, purpose has always been a stimulus and strength toward a single ideal world, and you must understand this fact.  
Therefore, the closer the world gets to the ideal world, the conclusion arises that the purpose desired by all people must move toward a single goal. From this perspective, when you look at the current world situation, you can see that it is moving toward a single ideal world.  
The Path of Purpose  
Currently, the world is in conflict between the democratic world and the communist world. The purposes of democracy and communism are intertwined with human history, advancing and retreating in turn.  
So, what will happen? There cannot be two purposes. There cannot be an absolute purpose, the highest ideal purpose, that truly aligns with God's ideals. Therefore, the purposes of democracy and communism must ultimately become one. Today, democracy proclaims its ideals and principles, while communism does the same, but the reality is that we cannot deny that there is a struggle to find a direction for a purpose that can reach a single conclusion. We feel that the world has entered a stage where it can finally converge within a single ideal realm through the historical process and modern civilization of the 20th century.  
Then, were the consciences of our ancestors not good? They were indeed better than the present. Did the ideals that our ancestors envisioned fall short of the present? They certainly did not. Then why could they not assert a single ideal that could unify everything at that time? It is because there is a path for purpose. Purpose does not come to fruition all at once upon starting. There is a necessary process to go through to reach that destination.  
From a religious perspective today, it is undeniable that humanity's progenitor fell. So, what is the fall? It is the loss of the original direction that purpose can aim for, that is, losing the right direction toward which purpose should go. It is going down paths that should not be taken while leaving aside the paths that should be taken. In other words, it is abandoning the direction that aligns with purpose and going in the opposite direction, which is the fall.  
Therefore, we cannot help but acknowledge that human history began with the fall of humanity's progenitor. Thus, humanity must turn back and navigate toward a single ideal world.  
What then did the many prophets and sages who have traversed the historical process do? They each put forth their assertions to try to unify the tangled directions of purpose into a single direction. They sought to establish a single ideological goal to resolve the tangled directions of purpose. Furthermore, they were people who found paths that could align with a single absolute ideal world. Then, how did they align those paths? Did they align them on parallel lines or straight lines? In any ideology or assertion, if you align it by one degree, the remaining distance will still have trials left. Depending on the angle from which you start and how far you go, you will know your mission until the end of the connections that occur in the historical process. Thus, the angle of trials decreases accordingly.  
From this perspective, what has emerged to move toward a higher goal centered around conscience? Philosophy is one, but religion has dealt with this even more deeply. Therefore, when we overview human history up to now, culture has developed through a religious foundation. In other words, the development of culture has been guided by a religious foundation through a long historical process, bringing the cultural realm of that era into a single direction. Why was that? It was to resolve toward a single purpose that purpose aims for.  
The Purpose That Purpose Aims For  
The significant mission in directing purpose is religion. The deeper the history of such religion, the deeper and newer content emerges that can surpass the cultural world of reality. Thus, the standards of purpose through that religious content or ideological standards must be linked to the purpose that all humanity aims for. So, what is democracy centered on today? It is Christian thought. However, communism has an opposing ideology.  
When tracing the path of purpose, purpose cannot escape its essence. Purpose is connected through the comprehensive best standards, so to reach a conclusion, it cannot be achieved in a short time. Moreover, to connect that relationship, it must relate to human history and cultural history. From this perspective, the religion that has contributed to the development of purpose while taking on significant responsibilities and missions in reality is Christianity.  
But where did communism come from? It emerged suddenly around 50 years ago, in 1917, centered on the Soviet Union.  
Can this communism unify all historical purposes and all the purposes of the current era? It cannot.  
When your conscience bows to a true, conscientious conscience, is the higher standard materialistic or idealistic? Without a doubt, it is idealistic. A person with a lot of money is not called a person of character. A person of character must possess something greater based on their conscience.  
Therefore, in reality, a new form must be established centered on the history of religion. And it must have a system of thought that leads the way forward. Furthermore, it must determine the direction of humanity based on Christian thought. From this perspective, we can see that communism is going in the opposite direction of purpose.  
The purpose of purpose is to seek ideals. Through what is the ideal achieved? It cannot be said that simply eating three meals a day and being full constitutes an ideal.  
So, what is the purpose that purpose aims for? It is not being full from eating. Moreover, no matter how much a person loves alcohol, alcohol cannot be the purpose. So, what is more problematic? It is love. That love is not temporary love, nor is it a few pennies' worth of love that can be bought cheaply. It is essential love.  
When analyzing this essential love, we can see that there is no revolution in love. A parent's love for their child corresponds to true love. Therefore, the heart that a person had for their child from the time of humanity's progenitor is the same as the heart that we, thousands of years later, have for our children. Likewise, the hearts of our descendants thousands of years later will also be the same. Love does not develop or end. It is pure love that does not require the conditions of revolution.  
Then, what is God's love? If God places an absolute being in the position of a standard and acknowledges their existence and loves them, that love does not require revolution anymore.  
To fulfill purpose,  
Where does revolution start? It starts from desire. If there is something bad, it must be discarded, and good content must be applied in front of the whole. It must be applied to society to create a revolution in society, applied to religion to create a revolution in the religious realm, and applied to all other fields to initiate revolutions in those areas.  
What purpose aims for is ideology. However, ideology alone cannot fulfill purpose. Purpose must be resolved through the issue of love. In other words, to fulfill purpose, material cannot be used.  
From this perspective, what Christianity emphasizes most is love. So, what is the method to achieve this love? It is to pair the bride and groom. Throughout the long historical process, what has emerged centered on the content of love is Christianity. Therefore, Christianity could not help but become a global religion.  
So, what must Christianity do now? To achieve its ideals, it must become a global religion, and to become a global religion, it must bring forth the issue of love. At this time, that love must have validity. That love should not only apply to Abel and not to Cain, or only to the people of South Korea and not to the people of the United States. The history that has gone through revolutions until now must be able to integrate and adapt in an instant. If Christianity has such love, it can unify the nations of the world centered on Christianity and create an ideal world. However, when that love is lacking, a new revolution must occur within Christianity.  
The more we look at Christianity until now, the darker it seems. When we trace back the environment from the current point, we can see that the content that can connect to the present point is unclear. The form is established, but there is nothing to boast about in terms of content.  
Generally, climbing a tree is more difficult than coming down. However, when climbing a really tall tree, it may be somewhat easy to go up, but coming down is more difficult. Also, even if one has come down, when trying to go back up, there are many cases where they cannot go back up. However, if one has come down, they must go back up.  
Love also  
Ah! Do I just keep saying I love you and keep going up? No, that’s not it. Love must go up and down, give and receive. Therefore, love cannot be done alone. The relationship between a loving father and son transcends the distance even if they are at the ends of the earth and seeks each other out to embrace and love one another. What is the cause of this? It is love.  
God is an absolute being, and we are extremely humble beings. But how can we, humble beings, love God? An absolute being cannot come and go to a humble place. Therefore, Christianity has come down to this point with the mission of connecting to that standard and has gained a global character. So, how will this be done? It must be universalized and applied to the public laws of love that all people can truly recognize.  
To do this, it must be able to transcend the historical process of the current era.  
The Time for Love to Emerge
So what is the mission that Christianity must undertake in the future? It must fulfill a religious mission to achieve an ideological purpose that is comprehensive of historical processes. Therefore, we must ascend following the historical connections that have been passed down and then descend again. It took 6,000 years to descend, but it should not take another 6,000 years to ascend again. Why? Because life is short. No matter how long a person lives, they can only live for a hundred years. However, if we are to trace back through 6,000 years of human history, it would take 6,000 years, and it would also take 6,000 years to descend again.

Thus, this must be shortened, but what can achieve that? It is love centered on truth, even more than the truth itself. That love transcends time. The love for a child who died ten years ago is similar in that it transcends time. What is the absolute factor that can transcend historicality and allow for interaction? It is love, not truth. Jesus taught his disciples the truth, but that truth was merely a means to teach love. Therefore, he could not fully realize the activities that could accomplish love. Because of this, the content of love through actionable results could not be introduced, and this has been the history of Christianity up to today.

Thus, at this point in time, a new ideology that aims for a new purpose must emerge, one that can integrate and complete countless ideologies to create happiness for humanity. What kind of ideology is that? It is a love-centered ideology that can traverse concrete history and the times. Because God desires such an ideology, He sent His beloved child, that is, His son, to wear the crown of the bridegroom and to establish all people who follow His will as brides. Therefore, even though history flows, the connections of heart are always flat. Thus, while we have traversed vertical history, God governs the flat, realistic stage of that society, so Christianity must become a practical religion and a social religion. In this light, what kind of church is the Unification Church?

When the first humans, Adam and Eve, fell, did they fall while receiving God's love or without receiving it? Here, God is the Father of humanity, so He must have loved Adam and Eve, but why did they fall without receiving God's love? This raises a question. God's love for Adam and Eve cannot be without a special path; it cannot be a vague love. Even if there are a hundred sons, there is only one son who can inherit the father's legacy.

From this perspective, to establish a system of love in this fallen world, we must have a chosen people ideology centered on God. You are the collateral relatives, and we are the direct descendants. A capable nation must emerge. Love is the same. The teacher must be able to love all of you at once. Therefore, one must be able to go directly and must be willing to dedicate all their possessions and even their life. In other words, one must become a person who can transcend life and death for the sake of that one ideology and love, the only love. Then, among the fallen people, who becomes the heir of love? It is someone who stands in the position of Adam before his fall. The concepts of chosen people and so forth arise because love has gone wrong.

To find God's love, from this perspective, it is necessary that a person who can fulfill God's will to teach the principles of love must arise within the realm of the fallen. Therefore, the ideology of the chosen people must emerge through the Israelite nation.

Israel means victory. What did they win against? Was it a victory in some sporting event? Or was it a victory in loving the bride? No, it was the first victory in seeking God's love. So how should we go about seeking God's love? Can we find it by following the ways of the world? No, we must not follow the people of the world. We must go the opposite way from the people of the world, the way that opposes Satan. Thus, Noah, Abraham, and Jacob all left their homes and packed their bags.

To walk the path of the will, one must desire God's will more fervently than anyone else. Therefore, today we must deny the world itself. We must strike against the world. In other words, religion must deny the present world and overcome philosophy.

Then what kind of group is the one that vehemently denies the present world? It is the Christians who have a history of martyrdom. They are the ones who, in order to fulfill God's will and eliminate the ills of society, have cried out while denying society even as they faced martyrdom. This Christianity has completely denied the present world, which is why it has been driven away from society. Because it has vehemently denied society, it has faced intense persecution and has been driven away. When one denies the present world, they will inevitably face persecution from society. Thus, Christianity has been driven away, chased, and persecuted.

But why do those who persecute perish while those who are persecuted do not perish? It is because those who are persecuted have a connection to the direction of the will and possess a heart that can resonate with that will, loving heaven, loving the earth, and loving the ideals of the future. In other words, they have established a connection that can align with heavenly fortune, so even if the people of the world perish, they do not perish and remain.

Therefore, when the day comes when the principles of heart that can unify the democratic world and the communist world through a religious ideology centered on the loving God are revealed, the world will automatically unify. It cannot be unified through military talks or peaceful discussions.

On this planet, nearly 3 billion people live. Among them, nearly 2 billion live within religious cultural spheres. Thus, two-thirds of the world's population lives within religious cultural spheres. Can communism penetrate this religious sphere? It cannot.

Therefore, a new religious movement must emerge. In this context, Unification Church members must appear as global princes with a new ideology and thought. If all humanity has religion, communism will crumble like dust. Then, we must integrate the intertwined history and the remaining history to find a resolution.

So who will become the master? On the surface, it may seem that those who rob and assault are the masters, but that is not the case. The true master is the one who loves people more than anyone else. Even dogs follow those who love them. A person without a loving heart cannot become a master.

The Conclusion of Human History
The Communist Party drives humanity into death through violent politics and coercive politics. They do everything at night, never during the day. Their operations all take place in the dark. There is nothing done during the day. Night is a shadow. Shadows must perish. Therefore, the Communist Party must perish.

From this perspective, what is the substance that can sustain the world in the future, considering the purpose of the will? It is not material. It is historical love that has bled, shed tears, and groaned with history, longing for the day of reconciliation with history. Therefore, a leader who embodies that historical love must emerge on this earth. Who is that leader? In Christian terms, it is the Messiah.

Based on this content, humanity must live according to God's will after preparing to welcome the Messiah who will come as the bridegroom. Those who consider themselves intellectuals may say that religion is unnecessary, but that is not the case.

So what does the Unification Church want to do? At this point, we want to feel God's love. How much must we feel God's love? The love that has existed throughout the historical process is not enough. We cannot rely on the power of that love. The vague love that Jesus advocated 2,000 years ago is not sufficient. It must be a more precious love, a valuable love, a substantial love, and an empirical love. It must be stronger than anything else, and we must have the attitude to feel God's love more strongly than anyone else with a realistic mindset.

How can we feel love strongly? First, we must understand how the path of love has been laid out. How can we know that parents love their children? The love between a husband and wife cannot be understood merely through words. A child feels their parents' love by tracing back the path of their parents' love for them and finally realizing, "Ah! My parents were such people!"

Now, let us trace back and recall that love. How ideal must the love that began centered on God be? If humanity had not fallen, that love would have started as a magnificent and beautiful love. God's heart was one that lived intoxicated in the freedom of the universe, dreaming of that beautiful love. However, that heart of God was suddenly hit by a whirlwind and froze suddenly like ice. The heart of God, which had been swelling with love like a hot fire, felt an explosive sorrow when ice was poured onto it. Therefore, we must seek that love again. The history of humanity up to now has been a restoration movement to find that love.

What is the conclusion of human history? It is simple. It is a movement to find the original love centered on God. To find that love, humanity has flowed through history, varying methods, means, forms, and concepts, but the purpose has always been one.

God's Love
Today, when I look at myself, what relationship does God's love have with me? In practical terms, it has no relationship. How deep must that relationship be? One must feel a relationship deeper than that between Jesus and the Israelite nation. If not, one cannot feel Jesus' love. Do you understand what I mean? In other words, one must have a heart that can love Jesus more than the disciples who followed him.

The Unification Church must historically clarify these matters. That is, it must explain how love has developed historically. Through the evidential facts clarified historically, we must establish a standard in our lives that says, "Because history is like this, I must be like this, and because history is like this, I have this value socially." Such a life itself is loving God and standing in a position of loving Jesus. If anyone can understand that content, the world will automatically unify.

There is no need for means or methods here. Even in a family, when a loving wife cooks, the food tastes better. Also, when a mother cooks, it tastes good for no reason. A mother with children does not find her child ugly, no matter how dirty they get. Rather, they are cute and lovable. Isn't that so?

God's love is well manifested in the historical process. When we look at any nation, even those who have been persecuted and chased in fierce struggles, when they lose their lives, they can re-establish the sovereignty of their nation and make a new start because God's love for humanity has been behind them. Even in the history of countless nations rising and falling, in the historical process of Christianity that changes with each era, and in today's process of global cultural exchange and conflict, God's love is always present. Even if the society of the Republic of Korea is corrupt, there is God's love hidden there that we do not know about.

When we see this, even in this corrupt Republic of Korea, there is a person who can contribute to the world, and that is God's love. Therefore, you must understand that God's love is even more present in this corrupt world. And you must feel that this love of God is for the purpose of saving this world.

Thus, Christianity must go out and shout love while holding onto the evil world. However, Christianity has not been able to develop such content and therefore has no destination. A religion that cannot save society and has lost the ability to lead society is declining.

This cannot be achieved through any structured form or foundation. It must be a natural attitude of conscience that flows from the bones, and when that power aligns with heavenly fortune and finds the emotions that can traverse history, there human transformation and human recreation will occur.

Therefore, people must be revived, but they must not be revived through means and methods. The more conscientious a person is, the more they wish to be revived through absolute truth. However, what they desire even more deeply in their hearts is to be revived through true love. Why is that? Because when people die, they want to die in the arms of someone they love and in an environment filled with love. It is not in a place where they have piled up gold and treasures, but in a place where they gain trust through a loving heart that divine connections are established.

Love is what everyone likes.
Today, when we say we have religion, it means that we must be able to carry out a reform movement for society. A religion that does not have the explosive heart to do so cannot fulfill its mission. Religion has silently presented new environments until now. No matter how evil a nation may be, if we throw a bomb of true love at that nation, they will surely melt and assimilate.

Your hearts are the same. I know from growing up in the countryside that a calf tied with a rope is very difficult to lead before it has a nose ring. However, when you take the calf and make a bamboo stick to put through its nose and pull the lead, the calf will bleed from its nose and be led away. From that point on, you can lead the calf without much effort. However, even if the calf has a nose ring, it will not follow someone who does not love it. Only someone who loves that calf can easily lead it.

What will be able to digest the world in the future? It is neither communism nor democracy. It is love. However, love cannot be just the love of a parent for their child. It cannot be a love that does not feel sorrow for the death of someone else's child. Moreover, when a man and a woman love each other, if they are only good with each other, that love has nothing to do with the people of the world. So what kind of person is needed? A person who can live with fairness and equality in an absolute world is needed.

What do people in the world desire? To make a lot of money, right? So people leave their hometowns to earn money, but soon they think, "Oh, I need to return to my hometown." Why do they want to return to their hometown? Because they miss the mountains and rivers of their hometown. They want to be embraced by their loving parents. That is why when they see food, they unconsciously shed tears. Also, just thinking of their hometown makes their hearts swell, and they feel a sense of longing as if they are seeing a spring meadow. Why is this? Because there are loving connections with their parents and siblings in their hometown.
I want to find and go. In other words, I miss the love of my parents and the bond with my siblings. 

Everyone, let’s quietly think about the word family. What does the character for family (家庭) signify? It signifies ‘courtyard.’ Just as various beautiful flowers bloom in the courtyard, there are siblings and parents in the family. So, should those flowers create a courtyard that loves each other, or should it become a bad courtyard where they dislike each other? A family should be a place where everyone can rejoice, enjoy, sing, and dance together. But what happens if they fight there? It becomes a wasteland. Everything is ruined. 

If a child takes a few coins from their father’s pocket out of greed for money and puts it in their own wallet, that child is foolish. They should not do that. Material things are limited. They cannot transcend their limitations. However, the bundle of love, when opened, is infinite. 

Therefore, when viewed from the center of love, the love of parents, the love between spouses, the love of children, the love of kin, the love of a nation, the love of the world, and the love of the universe all have different standards. The fact that they are different means that everyone can appreciate them. 

Plants grow well when they listen to good music, but they do not grow properly when they hear bad music. You should try this experiment. Thus, if you engage in fights and listen to useless noise, you will become like plants that do not grow well. However, if you listen to songs that are imbued with love, you can live beautifully. What allows you to live beautifully is the heart filled with love. 

The path of purpose is the path of love. 

Do you know why adolescence is wonderful? It is because it is wonderful. During adolescence, one often feels a lack of appetite and throws away their studies. They are always excited and worry that they might fly into the sky like a satellite. How wonderful would it be if that could happen? 

What is the highest purpose of humanity? What is the desire? Humans want to cling to the earth and live on it, but ultimately, where do they go? They go to the grave. However, humans long for the embrace of a mother filled with love, for the embrace of siblings with whom they can share love, and for the embrace of a beloved spouse. Nothing can block love. Therefore, the highest truth is to go forth centered on love. 

This proves that Christianity cannot help but be a global religion. Such content does not exist in Buddhism. It does not exist in Confucianism either. 

Jesus spoke about the bride and groom, and also about brothers. In other words, the pinnacle of the universe is that all humanity is one family. Therefore, humanity must seek a love that prioritizes the family over oneself, a love that seeks the kin over the family, a love that seeks the nation over the kin, and a love that seeks the world over the nation. That is the path of purpose, and it is the path of love. 

A loyal subject must disregard their own personal interests, their own family, and their own kin for the sake of the nation. That is the duty of a loyal subject. Likewise, a filial child must disregard their own self, their own spouse, and follow the will of their parents. That is the duty of a filial child. Therefore, the path of purpose is the path of love. The path of loving greater things than oneself is the path of purpose and the path of love. 

From this perspective, when we consider the universe, Jesus had to become the Messiah of all people. Even while being pierced by the spears of enemies on the cross, mocked and ridiculed, even in that most unjust and miserable moment of death, he prayed, “Father, forgive them.” (Luke 23:34) 

Thus, we must have a love that surpasses the love of Jesus, and we must be able to love not only those connected to us but even our enemies. Furthermore, we should not only like the light but also have the capacity to appreciate the dark powers of pitch-black darkness. Only then can the love of God, which can repel the evil forces behind it, dwell within us. 

If that happens, we can create a global cultural world centered on Christianity. However, such facts do not manifest outwardly. The desire and faith of the Unification Church is to clarify this content. 

Therefore, you must have a heart that can love the family more than yourself, the kin more than the family, the nation more than the kin, the world more than the nation, and heaven and earth more than the world. Furthermore, you must have a heart that can love God more than heaven and earth. This is the heart that God desires. 

God has many desires. Six thousand years ago, God set the standard of love before humanity and commanded them to love only Him. This is a universal principle, not a dictatorship. Jesus also said that if one does not love him more than anyone else, they are not worthy of him and cannot be his disciple. Because there is a universal principle, there is also a standard of love. Through this process, the heavenly fortune moves history, so God allows humanity to pray in advance, sparing them from suffering. That is why, although it is tedious, He makes humanity endure for thousands of years. 

Therefore, God has raised those who desire to be blessed, telling them to die and die again, while guiding them to uphold the will of heaven and earth. Was that good or bad? It was good. 

The path of purpose is the path of ideals. 

The teacher of the Unification Church wants to make God my God. I do not want Him to be someone else's God. This desire is not a sin; it is a virtue. If the teacher makes God my God and loves you, you should also be pleased. However, the country that the teacher wants to love the most opposes him the most. It is a shocking situation. 

The path of purpose is the path of ideals. Ideals must be established centered on love. Only then can a foundation of eternal rest be established there. However, until now, no environment has been created where one can rest eternally. Therefore, religious people must go toward that place from a position of possibility. However, there seems to be no religious person who thinks they are going from a position of possibility. The Unification Church must believe in possibilities and feel them as they go. Are you feeling that? If you do not feel it, you must pack your bags again and seek it out. The teacher must also pack his bags again and seek it out. 

To love only God and to love only the Lord is both a motive for love before humanity and a fruit of it. That is why Christianity has sacrificed itself over the long history of two thousand years and has survived until now. 

Everyone, the end is drawing near. The final finishing line is approaching. It is time to score a goal. Therefore, when there is only one last step left, do not stand back and watch, saying, “I have run enough… You guys are just now coming.” Even if that person has run a thousand miles, they must understand that they can still go many more miles with that last step. 

At the end, Christianity has reached the final finishing line where it can govern the world and score a goal, yet they are resting. In other words, Christianity can have the authority of victory that it can boast of before the universe, yet they are resting at the finishing line. While resting, they realize, “Oh, where am I? I didn’t notice this while running, but something else has attached itself here,” and they lose sight of their original purpose and engage in other activities. However, the Unification Church must be different from current Christianity. It must not be the same. 

Then, what is the path of purpose in the present? It is the path of goodness. What is goodness? Is it fulfilling one’s own desires? Is it snatching what is in someone else's wallet? No, it is giving. It is being saturated with a heart of love. However, love goes beyond this saturation point. While saturation cannot rise beyond that point, love breaks through and surpasses that standard. We, the members of the Unification Church, must connect our activities through love to God’s heart, forming a bond that brings joy to God. 

Life must seek the original love. 

Billions of people are born centered on love and die centered on love. In other words, people are born in love, live centered on love, and die in love. Thus, people rely on unchanging love to live and find rest where unchanging love dwells. Therefore, if it is a place where such love dwells, even in a crevice of rock, one can stretch out and comfortably take a nap. 

You were born by your parents' love, right? If you were born of true love, you should hold onto love and live in a true world. That is the ideal life. However, because humans were born through the intersection of wrong love, they end up living in a realm of wrong love and dying in that wrongness. Therefore, humanity must reclaim the original love. 

We must undergo the resurrection that Christianity speaks of. Because we were not born in the original love, did not live in the original love, and could not die in the original love, we must carve a path to be reborn, to live again, and then to die. Our lives must be a journey to reclaim the original love. 

What is the path of original love? It is the path where ideals can dwell. Then what are those ideals? They are the ideals of creation that God had when He originally created humanity. Love is the most mysterious thing. 

Humans do not rest even after conquering God. All men are thieves. The teacher is also a man, and this cannot be denied. Just because one has conquered God does not mean they are satisfied or happy. What does human desire want to conquer? It desires the heart of God, the secret treasure in the center of His heart. Once one completely conquers this eternal love, human desire will then fall away. Humans are warriors who have entered the competition to conquer God's love. 

Until now, the teacher has faced insults and heard all sorts of rumors in South Korea. However, if the rumors circulating are seen as a problem by the people of the world, it establishes the conditions to conquer them, so it is not a bad thing. That is why the teacher is enduring the difficult path and leading the Unification Church. In other words, one must boldly overcome the severe persecution and suffering from the evil world led by Satan to become an indispensable person. 

From a worldly perspective, a seemingly worthless woman enters the Unification Church and prays for others. Within their hearts, there is a desire to forgive others with love and hope for love, wanting to dwell forever in that love. However, if someone tries to steal that love, that person is a thief of love. Does God dislike that? God also appreciates it. The greatest thief of love is God Himself. (Laughter) 

If someone says, “Oh, hardworking God! Love me,” they will soon forget love. Forgetting is not eternal possession. Humans must originally live in God's love and die in God's love. No matter how much the teacher has suffered, he has endured because he knows he must die on this path. 

No matter how much we may appear to be living off scraps, we will not perish. Is it a sin to eat a few meals to repay God's enemies? One can do even greater things than that. You must understand this. When the teacher was in Busan, he worked at the docks and earned money, but his purpose was different from that of others earning money. The teacher can do anything. He can even sort salt at a salt field very well. There is hardly anything he has not done. He has also farmed. You should all try these things. 

The teacher is a person with not a single penny, yet he has never envied anyone in the world. He did not even envy the President of the United States. (Omitted) 

In difficult times, the teacher never prays to God. He does not play games like asking for help when in trouble and saying goodbye when things are good. 

The standard of love established by the Unification Church. 

You may be wearing clothes and living proudly, but all of that is just temporarily borrowed. In other words, your life is like that of a traveler, and the house you live in is nothing more than an inn or hotel. We have infinite value. How pitiful it is that we cannot hear the call that beckons us? 

People must be born in love, live in love, and die in love. What is that love? It is not a love that comes and goes for money. It is the love that ignites the origin of existence, governs the story of existence, and realizes the fruits of existence. This love is absolute from birth until death. That is why people want to unify the world and want to sit on the throne, boasting before all people and simultaneously wanting to live with those they love. Up to this point is human desire. 

However, the desire of the Unification Church goes one step further. The desire of the Unification Church is not just the love of two, but to combine the love of two and have God dwell among them, achieving Godism and bringing all 3 billion people into that. Thus, it aims to establish the original world, binding humanity around God and loving everyone. That is the love that the Unification Church seeks to establish. 

Do you understand? 

That is why Jesus sought to restore the world centered on Christianity. Therefore, now the world is within the Christian realm and acknowledges the love of Jesus. Christianity has come forth from two thousand years ago until now, seeking to resurrect humanity, placing God among them, and binding humanity to God to create a garden of love. This is the kingdom of heaven on earth and the first ideal of Christianity. 

Then, how do we explode the emotional love that prioritizes horizontal relationships over bloodline relationships? Until now, humanity has followed the path of vertical love. However, we have not been able to develop that vertical love into the world. That is why the world is in chaos. Therefore, a new bundle of love that can separate this vertical love, respecting that love, must be unraveled. In other words, one must love all of humanity more than their own spouse, more than their own children. 

From God's perspective, all humanity is equal. The children I love and all of humanity are equal before God. Therefore, those who wish to bear the responsibilities and missions they can carry and desire to love more precious and valuable beings are on God's side. Thus, such...
To develop love, one must love the world beyond their own relatives, tribes, and nations. Jesus was a person who loved the world beyond nations. That is why Jesus becomes the Lord of the world, and humanity must restore this world centered on Jesus. 

The path of purpose is the path of love and goodness. The path that purpose takes is the path of ideals. However, this path of purpose has become a path of suffering. What is the ideal of God, the Creator? It is for humans to be born in love, live in love, and die in love. Those who walk this path of life will forever become the masters of that love and that path, while those who do not will all flow away. Therefore, humanity must have such love. 

So what about Unification Church members? It means to live again in love and die in love. It is not just the love of my family, but to hold onto the love of heaven and earth while living and dying. Originally, the hope of the human ancestors, Adam and Eve, was to unite heaven and earth. They were born for that purpose. Today, humanity should also be born in such love and live to practice that love, but humans do not even know this. 

Thus, God sent Jesus as the Second Adam to inherit the bond of love and to practice that love. For this purpose, He established the nation of Israel. However, because the nation of Israel lost the foundation of that love by not believing in Jesus, God moved the stage of activity back to the spirit world. Therefore, Jesus will come again to spread that love globally, and that day is the day of Jesus' Second Coming. In other words, Jesus will return to create one world with the love that God desires. 

So where will that love go? The path that love takes is the path that goodness takes, and the path that purpose takes. Therefore, you must have a love that can place the family before the purpose, even if it means sacrificing yourself. It means sacrificing the small for the sake of the great. You must become a love that can develop global love, even if it means sacrificing your personal love. When such people begin to emerge on this earth, then the ideal world of the heavenly kingdom will begin to be realized. Do you understand? 

For those who have come here for the first time, you may not know much about the Unification Church, right? The Unification Church is a church that the Republic of Korea dislikes. But who says they know? Is there a reason to say the Unification Church is bad? Those who first came to the Unification Church thought, "Wow, this is amazing! Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is incredible!" However, there are people who criticize it without knowing what kind of church it is. Those people have been living off the country while focusing on their own families, using the nation for their own benefit and sitting on great things. 

It is not filial piety but loyalty. Isn't that right? One must serve their parents with all their filial devotion, not abandon them to walk the path of loyalty. Therefore, on the path of purpose, one absorbs and sacrifices the smaller values for the greater value. Then unity will be achieved. Is unity good or not? "It's good." Then why do established church members hate the Unification Church? The head is unity, and the bottom is the church, so they are cousins... 

Everyone! Can you promote it? You don't know how to promote it, do you? So, the opposing winds must come together and intertwine to achieve unity. Do you understand? "Yes." 

How should unity be achieved? You must follow the purpose. If you are told to love Americans more than Koreans, would you feel upset? You would feel upset, but you must save Western people even if it means sacrificing Koreans. And even if it means cutting the hair of the aunties to make wigs to sell, you must help foreigners. How about that? You would feel upset, right? Why are you just sitting still? How far must you go? You must go to the very bottom where you could die. It’s a big deal, right? Otherwise, you cannot become a globalist. 

The Unification Church teaches the way to become a globalist. A little while ago, a Japanese girl came, and she trusts Korean people and leaves her money at the headquarters church. She did not go to her uncle's house in Korea but came to the Unification Church in Korea with just a handbag. What power does Reverend Moon of the Unification Church have? However, when it comes to eating, he eats with the great composure of someone hosting a 60th birthday party in his own home, surrounded by daughters-in-law and grandchildren. Who taught him to do that, even he does not know. 

Even if you want to kill your worst enemy, you must love them and keep putting in the principles. What we carry today is such a principle. Therefore, Unification Church members are different from people in the world. That is why they receive a lot of criticism. However, even when others point fingers, the teacher has devoted himself wholeheartedly to informing the world of the purpose while silently shedding tears. 

Tears for humanity, sweat for the earth, blood for heaven. Now the teacher is about to leave Korea and go abroad. To save foreign people, he will take the Unification Church members with him. If all of humanity can be saved, the teacher would be willing to die. Is this a sin or a good deed? "It is good." Then I will take you with me. The teacher has never once complained to God. Yet, he has led you all this way. Along the way, he has been in and out of prison many times. Now he is a doctor who knows everything about prison. He has endured many cruel beatings there. That is why if he were to hit someone, he could do it pitifully. Handling one person while walking down the street is not a problem. He can do it confidently and silently. 

Whatever the teacher decides to do, he can accomplish it within three years. You may have tried to resolve your grievances secretly, but the teacher has already experienced all of that. Saying this, how do you feel? "Good." Why is it good? Do you like the teacher from the perspective of being a fellow Korean, or do you like him from God's perspective? "Both." (Laughter) You think the teacher is bad, right? He subtly pretends to be God's agent, so you must feel bad about that. 

In the global struggle, until now, the Unification Church has lost. In the first half of the war, the Unification Church was destined to lose. However, in the second half, it will win. The standard of victory will be surpassed. That is why many people are needed. (Omitted) 

The teacher cannot only operate in Korea. He must also work in the United States, Germany, and Japan. He has the determination to restore everyone there someday. Once a bee that has tasted honey sticks to a board covered in honey, it will not fall off no matter how hard you try to pull it away. Similarly, once someone tastes the sweetness of God's love, they will be willing to dedicate their own nation to God's will. They will desperately strive to restore it. What is the most important thing in taking charge of the world, humanity, and nations? It is God's love. Even if you live starving, it is good if there is love. 

Everyone, you said you would be okay with being taken away, right? Is that really true? Jesus also walked that path. The teacher has also walked that path and has faced many trials. You must understand that. (Omitted) 

Among those here, there may be people who came from established churches. They probably tested the Unification Church a lot at first to see if it had substance or not. They would have hit it to see if it was ripe or not. After testing, they would find it is very ripe. If those people come to know the taste of the Unification Church, if they taste the spring garden-like flavor of the Unification Church, children to grandmothers will line up waving their hands to come in. The world of the heart is like that. 

When you enter the Unification Church, who recognizes you? God recognizes you. The teacher works according to God's strategy. You must not live for your own sake. You must save this nation. Therefore, tears must be shed for humanity, sweat for the earth, and blood for heaven. 

Until now, I did not know, but now that I know the taste, it is so good. It is astonishing! You must feel the love of God to the fullest. 

Many have fallen away from the church due to not frequently receiving news from the church and being disconnected from it. You must become someone who can overcome any fierce wind that blows. Those who cannot do that are not Unification Church members. 

You must devote yourself to the path of purpose. 

Now the teacher must go abroad, but should I leave while blessing you or while cursing you? Should I take my affection with me or leave it behind? "Take your affection with you." The teacher must leave behind his affection. Think about it. If I take my affection with me, will Americans like it? Can a bride go to her in-laws with a messy appearance? Is that good? Is there anyone who can do that? Love is all the same. Therefore, the teacher must leave behind his affection from Korea. 

To detach what is attached, what must be done? If there are children following, they must be hit with a fist. If that does not work, they must be detached even with a knife. That is why it must be detached, but how to detach it? The teacher has always thought about this. You must think about it too. The teacher will make a full circle and forget all the stories that have happened until now. He wants to have a heart that starts anew. Do you understand? Until now, the teacher loved Korean people. But now he must leave them behind. Therefore, you must put in your sincerity and become one. (Omitted) 

You must come before the teacher with a bundle of your devoted sincerity and say, "This is all of it. Please take care of it." You must especially put in a lot of sincerity and pray. Do you understand? "Yes." Then how should sincerity be put in? Goodness follows sincerity, and the Father who granted the seven-year course has devoted seven years of sincerity unconditionally, so you must run day and night to put in more sincerity than that. Do you understand? It is not easy to put in such sincerity. 

In 1965, the teacher distributed the soil from the holy ground in Korea to 120 places around the world. In that process, he went to Japan to connect the lands of the world. However, in Japan, they said a crazy person had come when they saw the teacher. In fact, the teacher is indeed crazy. But the question is, what is he crazy about? He is crazy about establishing God's kingdom. 

So what must be done now? Once you are in a position to connect the lands, the next step is to connect the people. Among people, there are true people, those who put in sincerity. The teacher wants to connect the hearts of those who put in sincerity with the hearts of Unification Church members in a unified direction. For this, he will not hesitate to serve you at his own discretion. Therefore, you must pray centered on their sincerity. The teacher must go abroad and bless them. Everyone, do you know what blessing is? The teacher must bless. The hedonistic relationships of the power-seekers lead to a decisive state of defeat in life. However, women do not understand that. 

When the teacher goes to Japan, if he says he will not take any flight other than first class, the Japanese will sell their houses to buy him a first-class ticket and bring it to him. That is how it is. Our Unification Church is achieving things that ordinary people cannot understand. Now the teacher must travel the world and completely conclude the seven-year ordeal. Do you understand? "Yes." 

Therefore, you must put in your sincerity for the path of purpose. In other words, you must be prepared to sacrifice, to shed tears and sweat. You must be able to dedicate everything for the world in every aspect. 

The secret to restoring the world. 

For whom did God bless America? You must put in your sincerity with a heart that can align with God's heart, which loved America. This is what I am asking of you today. Do you understand? "Yes." Those who want to do that, raise your hands. If you raise your hands with such strength, the teacher will lose his confidence. Do you understand what I mean? If you put in your sincerity before the path the teacher takes, the teacher will surely repay you. While everyone else is criticizing this teacher, he cannot move against those who have devoted their sincerity, even while being pushed around. The teacher can maintain dignity in front of those who are not upright, but cannot do so in front of those who have put in sincerity. 

So what is the secret to binding God tightly? It is to turn around after being beaten and chased away, forget that beating, and go back to ask the Father for forgiveness, saying there was a reason for it. Therefore, one must become a person who can comfort that Father. When such a person exists, even a father like a scoundrel will have his heart melted. When such a person says, "Come here, Father," the father responds, "Yes, my son!" Such a person can bind God. When such a person binds God tightly, God will say, "It's okay to be bound tightly. Bind me even more." That is the secret to restoring the world. 

What I want to ask you is to pray and put in sincerity for the foreign family members scattered around the world, such as in Japan, America, and Germany, rather than praying for yourself on the path of purpose. You must be the ones who pray and put in sincerity for all of humanity. Do you understand? 

<Prayer> Father! I bow my head before you and reflect once again on the bitter path of history that you have walked. Please allow us to be sons and daughters who can pledge our filial devotion before you and remain in your heart. Father, who desires the path of purpose, the place where ideals reside, and where the ideal of creation is realized! Until now, the Unification Church has only played a role like the wind in the process of realizing that one ideal world that you desire. Why were we born as fallen humans on this earth? The mistake of that one day has left an unspeakable scar on the bodies and minds of the Unification Church members today, making our ancestors shed blood and struggle endlessly. We reflect deeply on this fact once again. We were miserable, but when we think about how much more miserable you must have been, we cannot help but bow our heads in repentance once again. 

Father, even if it means losing consciousness and collapsing to death, please allow us to be sons and daughters who long for you with a heart of longing that cannot endure without loving you. We are ashamed to be children who can offer all loyalty and sacrifice for the purpose of fulfilling your will, yet we did not know that you were longing for us. 

Children of unity, fearing that they might show their own joy before the Father, covering their faces and suppressing their joy, please allow them to be your children who strive to see the joyful appearance of Heavenly Father. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.
Father, please protect the land of Korea. Please love the children of unification scattered throughout Korea. In times of difficulty, it is essential to have someone who protects and comforts us. When I was in such times, you treated me that way, so I earnestly hope that you will protect the many children scattered across South Korea as well, Father.

Father, as a vanguard warrior standing before your will, please ensure that there is nothing in the reality that hinders our relationship. Centered on your complete love, I know that each individual is a precious brother who has received your bloodline, so let us be children who can share in your sorrow and know how to comfort. I earnestly wish that we become true filial sons and daughters who can bear your yoke and relieve it, Father.

Please allow the children gathered here today to return with something in their hearts. In this land where death surges, where the powers of darkness govern life, there are many obstacles and resistance from the enemy as a fragile candle of life desperately moves toward you, Father. I earnestly hope and wish that you will directly oversee and embrace us so that we can successfully break through to our desired destination.

Father, the children you have gathered here have already sworn before you. They have sworn a million times to dedicate their bodies and minds to you, so please allow them to offer their bodies cleanly before you. I earnestly wish that your children will strive to dedicate their bodies eternally before you and become sons and daughters who represent your love.

Please remember your many children who are worshiping here today, and embrace those who are praying with their hearts in anticipation of the day they will meet again, dreaming of this place while longing for it across the world, Father. I earnestly hope for this.

Although most of the environment has been self-centered, please comfort those who are within the realm of life that communicates with the same emotional feelings through their hearts. Please guide them to be children who are without lack before you, establishing them on the same purpose of desire and the same point of victory, Father. I earnestly hope and wish for this.

I earnestly ask that you be with everything that happens from this day forward. May your glory and love be with us forever. I have prayed in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
