Do not criticize others
<Summary of the Message> When the teacher was longing for the family members who would connect with God in Beomeo-dong, Busan, he waited for them with all his heart. Spiritually, they would come, but in reality, they were not coming close. So, there was nothing to do but wait for the time to come.

In Beomeo-dong, there were only three people, including the teacher. At that time, we lived with the mountains and rivers as friends while spiritually connecting.

When the teacher was 27 years old, if this doctor had united with the teacher, the will could have been fulfilled quickly; however, because that did not happen, the teacher went to the North.

The teacher's family does not need to establish conditions for indemnity. It must be dealt with one-on-one.

Now, no matter where the teacher goes, there are no wrinkles in his heart. This is because the will will be fulfilled even if the teacher dies. The number of Unification Church members is not the issue; rather, the question is how much of an environment is overall prepared for the will to be fulfilled.

The communist world will not surpass eight generations after Stalin, and from the seventh generation, it will go downhill.

May 14, 1967 (Sunday) Evening Service, former Headquarters Church.
* This message was given after the testimony of Mr. Ok Se-hyun, compiled from notes taken by former Association President Yoo Hyo-won and published in <Seonghwa> No. 66 (June 1967). The title was added by the editor.

Until now, material things have been the enemy for those engaged in spiritual history. However, from now on, things will change. If the economic issues that the teacher is concerned about are resolved well, then from that point, it will flourish.

The reason members lose grace is that they look at the senior members who have been active centered on the teacher from a critical perspective since the early days. Such people cannot develop any further. Those who walk the path of God's will should not criticize others until they have completed their own path. They should not criticize those who are uncovering the great events of heaven and earth.

The teacher walks this path with his life, so criticism from the side should not happen. Such people cannot gain strength no matter how hard they try. What the teacher does should be spoken of only after at least three years have passed. Since he cannot teach all the secrets of heaven directly, he speaks in parables and symbols.

People met through familial ties cannot be hated. Among members, there are two kinds of brothers, Cain and Abel, so if Cain criticizes Abel, he will lose grace.

---

Witnesses in Prison
<Summary of the Message> When three people on earth unite to slander one person, God withholds blessings from that person. If the person being slandered puts in more effort and loyalty than those slandering him, God will bless him even more.

When Jesus' disciples went to the spirit world, they could not go directly to Jesus. This was because they were slandered in the spirit world.

The reason saints on earth suffer is that they must indemnify and surpass the suffering that Jesus endured.

If you love a newly joined member, you can quickly establish conditions for indemnity. The reason the church does not develop is that the members do not do so. Therefore, God has told us to love and be harmonious with one another.

I wish to meet again those who went out while being loyal to the will in the past. This is because the initial motivation for meeting was the relationship between father and son. Although they may have opposed and left, the teacher must fulfill his responsibility. There are many enemies, but we cannot treat enemies as enemies because the purpose of the restoration providence is to save them under any conditions.

Even wicked people hope to be blessed and become good. The unforgivable person being forgiven and grateful will be greater than the one who can be forgiven and grateful. God conducts the work of salvation centered on that. Likewise, if Satan is forgiven, he will be able to show several hundred times the loyalty he had toward Adam in the past. The teacher has the heart to forgive even Satan after restoring everything.

If one goes too far in their service, indemnity follows, so the teacher does not make them do such things.

When I was in the North, the original date for my trial was April 3, but because the communists were trying to create an excuse to oppress the church, the date was delayed, and I received it on April 7. On that day, the members gathered together. However, from that time, they began to split.

When I was sentenced and went to prison, it was rather a hopeful step. This was because there would be people God had prepared even in the prison.

I entered the prison around 3 PM, and on the third day after entering, I met a young man named Kim. He had originally graduated from the Army Academy's artillery department and served as a Japanese army artillery captain when the war ended.

After the war, he joined the North Korean People's Army, serving as a trusted subordinate of the artillery commander, but he was sentenced to death for leaking state secrets and was just waiting for the day to die. He was also caught trying to commit suicide and was chained.

According to him, one day an old man with white hair appeared in his dream, calling his name and saying, "You will never die. You must prepare to welcome the young man who comes from the South to Pyongyang."

Soon after, under the absolute guarantee of the artillery commander, his punishment was reduced from death to four years and eight months. Then, in another dream, the old man appeared again, reproaching him for not believing and teaching him that he would meet the young teacher from the South in a few days.

Also, on the morning of May 28, when his beloved son was sentenced to death, he fell ill from grief, and to make matters worse, his father, who had died in a car accident, appeared in his dream and took him to a palace-like place.

There were stairs there, and every time he climbed the stairs, a new voice was heard, and as he climbed while bowing three times, there was a dazzling throne, and a young man sat majestically on it. His father said, "Look at that person," and when he looked up, the brilliance was so bright that he could not see clearly.

The cell the teacher entered was the same cell he was in. At that time, the teacher was 27 years old, and he was also 27 years old.

From the first moment he met the teacher, he felt drawn to him and had the impulse to hear the teacher's words, but it took three days for him to finally ask for the teachings.

The teacher shared the path he had walked until now under the alias Lawrence for three days. In doing so, he realized that there was someone promised by God here. That person was the cell leader, Mr. Kim.

The teacher asked him, "You have worries that you cannot share with anyone, right?" and in response, he was surprised and began to share everything that had happened, finally realizing that the young man he had seen sitting on the throne in his dream was indeed the teacher.

If you receive persecution with gratitude, you can take everything away from the persecutor.

Being in prison allows one to realize how good freedom is while also re-evaluating the value of everything.

The teacher has lived until now in a difficult spiritual atmosphere, like standing on the tip of a needle. However, now, wherever he goes, such things do not happen because the time has ripened.

---

Let the three become completely one
<Summary of the Message> The path of faith cannot be walked alone. Companions in faith are necessary. More than three must unite. Therefore, the need for the Trinity arises. God, who is the subject of human character, also hopes for three standards.

God cannot teach directly when humans make mistakes. However, while he cannot teach vertically, if three become one, even if one person makes a mistake, if the other two do not, they can teach that person’s mistake. This is the reason Jesus and the Holy Spirit were sent.

Even mountain prayers require three or more to receive grace quickly. After praying, they should discuss among themselves. However, if they discuss with others, Satan will invade.

When three people truly possess a beautiful appearance that can rely on each other, people around them will envy it, and when that happens, God's will will naturally multiply. Even without God's help, if the three become one, new sprouts will emerge from there.

When dealing with members, be careful not to hurt them and do not say anything that does not help their faith life.

If Jesus had united with his parents, he would never have died. Joseph and Mary were in the position of unfallen Adam and Eve, and Jesus was in the position of the original child.

When the teacher's heart is full, he looks for those who live graciously from a low position to speak to them. He does this because he must give to them. Sometimes, it has taken up to twelve hours to resolve a low spiritual state. Therefore, leaders must endure hardship.

It is a mysterious thing that the vast universe moves forward without colliding over a long history.

Do you have the power to give grace to others? Can you attract others? If you give completely, they will be drawn to you. However, if you give without meaning, it will consume more energy when trying to draw them in. Thus, if you only give without meaning, you will lose your faith. You must receive the power that comes from giving completely and having the other party respond joyfully.

The Trinity requires an older brother and a younger brother. You must receive from the older brother and give to the younger brother.

If you receive God's love, you must give that love, so you cannot avoid evangelism. To stand in the middle of serving God, you need those below you, which is why evangelism is necessary. There must be children of faith who can take responsibility for even your sins. Therefore, evangelism is not for the church but for yourself. When you convey the word with God's heart, it becomes evangelism.

If you have the ability to do good and align the hearts of the whole, you can become the center of the whole. Therefore, you must do good to many people and bestow grace. True goodness is wanting to share good things with all people. Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called children of God. Otherwise, you cannot become the center of the whole. Jesus' twelve disciples had to align the hearts of twelve people.

Since the original mind desires to develop, good things should be done after discussion among three. You must be able to share what you have received from God. It is more blessed to give than to receive.

A person who believes well should not love their own children. This is because God has not yet been able to love that child. If there is something to love more than your child, that is true. You must love God more than eating and sleeping, more than your children, and more than those you miss to enter the kingdom of heaven.

Before loving your own body, love what is around you. Only when you stand in the position of loving heaven, earth, and humanity can you stand in the original position of creation. Those who cannot govern material things cannot enter the kingdom of God. If you cannot love God more than your own body, you cannot enter heaven. This is the reason you cannot control your body as you wish.

The teacher is trying to establish material things because the time has come for the seven-year course to end. Those who possess what has not passed through parents are not family members. Family members must escape from the concept of ownership that it is theirs. Everything must be done in the name of the Father, and a relationship must be established where it can be redistributed from the Father. The teacher also does not think of his body as his own. If it is God's command, he can do anything.

Coming dressed in good clothes and showing off is like stabbing the hearts of the members. When one inevitably wears good clothes, they should feel sorry.

Among women, those who want to become the wives of the twelve apostles even in the spirit world must share their good clothes with more than twelve people.

We must be able to serve those who serve God.

---

Go the path of indemnity voluntarily
<Summary of the Message> A person feels the most miserable when parting from someone they love. The path of life is not always smooth. When a person faces a miserable situation, such as the death of parents or children, or separation from them, they are willing to do anything to recover from it. In such a situation, no one tries to elevate their own status. They try to be in the most humble and low position.

In such moments, 
"God, I will gladly receive the indemnity for the mistakes passed down from our ancestors. From now on, please accept this as an offering so that such things do not happen again." 
If you pray like this, you will transition into indemnity.
Do not think that you alone bear all the difficulties. Think that you bear them with God. If God does not feel sorrow, do not feel sorrow. It is useless to struggle not to receive in that position. 

At the moment Jesus died, it was determined whether the grievances of 4,000 years would be resolved or not. You cannot defeat Satan, who has rebelled for thousands of years, at that time. Because Jesus died, turning everything to the side of heaven and standing in the position that it is natural to receive forgiveness, the work of salvation came to pass. 

May 18, 1967 (Thursday), former headquarters church. 
* This message was given after the testimonies of Lee Bong-woon and Ji Saeng-ryeon, and it has been compiled from what former Chairman Yoo Ho-won recorded in his notebook and published in <Seonghwa> No. 66 (June 1967). The title was added by the editor.

When you voluntarily step into the path of restoration from the position of receiving blessings, you break free from the conditions of restoration you must establish for yourself, thus escaping from Satan's accusation rights. When that happens, Satan will be subdued. 

The Unification Church has walked the path of suffering, so the way ahead is open. Therefore, you may feel stagnant, but the Unification Church will grow globally and will subdue even the communist world. 

When a heavenly person joyfully receives restoration from the position of receiving blessings, blessings will come in proportion to that. If one goes out to evangelize by the word when it is not yet time to receive restoration and joyfully receives restoration, they can restore great things with small ones. A person who has received God's grace should not stop halfway. 

If a person who is in the position of having received all restoration stands in the position of joyfully receiving restoration, that will be established as a national level. 

To stand as an individual, one must restore their body. They must fight and win against their body. When one has completed familial restoration, they will stand in a position of victory in personal battles. To establish a familial position, one must win in tribal battles. Therefore, for the Republic of Korea to establish itself, it must establish itself to a global standard. Because of this, there may be things that are incomprehensible when viewed horizontally as we must establish a higher level. 

Sending you out for evangelism is a grace to help you restore. If a person who does not need to suffer, that is, a descendant of righteous ancestors, is struck by Satan, Satan will be ruined. Therefore, such a person cannot be struck by Satan. Rather, they should cooperate. 

You must know whether what is taught in the spirit world is a position of promise or a position that has achieved its purpose. In such a position, one must be humble above all. Therefore, one must analyze their own restoration journey. 

6)
Seek the New 
<Message Summary> A person who has received grace finds it hard to humble themselves. Therefore, God strikes them to bring them down, not by the same path they ascended, but through another path. 

To come down, one cannot rely solely on their own strength. Another force, that is, a second subject, is necessary. When one is in a high position, they must come down again, and if they cannot come down by their own strength, they must come down to a humble position through the children they have evangelized. 

The way to live in this path is to be despised and persecuted. Being persecuted while evangelizing is the way to live. Therefore, one must advance through evangelism. Evangelism must always be accompanied by restoration. One must establish conditions for restoration for evangelism to occur. Until the conditions for restoration are established, what comes before that easily belongs to Satan. If you can subdue three or more opposing people, evangelism becomes easy. It must be the time when the opposing person has been subdued for one to independently start. 

Reciprocal action is done to establish oneself. God created humans through reciprocal action to establish themselves. Therefore, to establish oneself, a center must be determined. 

When one is in a position where they cannot practice with their body, if they put in three times more sincerity with their heart, they will stand in the position of having acted with their body. If one does not feel more stimulating joy than before, they cannot develop. Therefore, one must provoke stimulating matters. 

Seek the new over the old. God starts from the new. God must operate above the new. You must equip yourself with a new personality. Until now, the teacher has pulled you along, but from now on, you must go on your own. No more can you be pulled along. And until now, the teacher has shed blood, but from now on, the teacher must not shed blood. 

Creation was done by God, but the standard of completion must be established by humans. However, humans have not achieved that standard of completion. The reason is that they have lost the word and heart. When one has the word and heart, the body is realized. When the heart stands on the foundation of the word, the entity is realized on top of that. The age of completion is realized centered on the heart. 

The first seven-year course is the era of individual restoration, but the second seven-year course is the era of family restoration, so it is more difficult. Therefore, one must have greater hope and be vigorous. One should have greater joy than when they joined the church. 

In the position elevated by God, one must feel all the labor of being raised and the labor of being brought down. Until now, the ascent was not done by oneself, but by God. Everyone is happy to ascend. However, despair comes when coming down. Nevertheless, in the path of following God, one must be able to rejoice even after losing everything of their own. That is because God did so. God came down to save the lost humans. Because one stands in the position of loving their enemies, the providence of restoration is fulfilled. Ultimately, it leads to the conclusion of suffering. 

The president may also be sent to a small church in the region. The teacher may not know how much joy it was when God raised them up. And the teacher was able to achieve victory because they were also joyful when sent down. Both ascending and descending are difficult, but only when one has completely come down can we experience God's heart. 

When the spiritual state falls, those who come to the teacher are all thieves. They come to steal because the door is open. At such times, one must pray on their knees. One must seek the new. A believer must always have a new feeling to develop. It must be new in development and new in descent. 

Seek the new 
Even though it is the same rice eaten every day, it is always new, so the flesh is revived. Even if one wears old clothes, they must always be new. Although the four seasons come every year, one must stand in the position of not having fully appreciated them yet. God is only a being whose range is large, and is not different from humans at all. 

If there is a person who has the opportunity to meet the Lord and the time has come, but that person has not met the Lord, they are taught to call him Lord. This is because at that time, God comes to find them. However, in fact, it is not that they are called Lord, but that it is said in reference to God who has come to find them. 

The purpose of holding this meeting today is to give you the joy you felt when you first saw the teacher, and also to let you know that Korea must leave to establish the new in order to prosper. 

The ultimate path, the path of death, is one that is walked alone. When death comes through restoration, it should be something to be thankful for; otherwise, one must be faithful until the end. Living the path of death is the path of religion. 

The teacher also often feels tired now. This is evidence of growing old. 

7)
Be Faithful in Prayer 
<Message Summary> One should pray for people rather than for material things. If one is to pray for material things, they should offer all their wealth and pray based on that condition. Also, if there is someone among relatives who lives conscientiously with material wealth, pray for them. If they are evangelized, the return of material blessings will naturally occur. 

The teacher does not worry about material things. The issue is how much sincerity you put forth before God for the factory. 

The path that family members must take has already been determined. If they walk that path, they will receive heavenly love. They must struggle to save the humans in the world of death. The teacher prayed for faith, wisdom, and love until the age of 30. The fall occurred because there was no faith and wisdom. At that time, Adam had love, but it was in an incomplete state. Because Adam and Eve fell from the position of parents, they must offer sacrifices from the position of parents. 

God's love is love for the world. The people of the world did not believe even after hearing this. But we should be able to say, "Is it because of such things that the will is not being fulfilled? If so, I will believe it." 

May 20, 1967 (Saturday evening), former headquarters church. 
* This message was given after the testimony of Jang Deok-hee, and it has been compiled from what former Chairman Yoo Ho-won recorded in his notebook and published in <Seonghwa> No. 66 (June 1967). The title was added by the editor.

To endure, one must experience God's love. 

The principle of the Unification Church is the principle of wisdom. 

The teacher's prayers are all public. There is no need for various prayers. The more one is a noun, the more they must aim accurately when holding a gun. Prayer should be like that. 

Do not regret the results of your sincerity. That is foolish and goes against the heavenly law. However, because you do it habitually, God cannot work. 

For difficult purposes, pray three times a day. Because it is a time of serving, if you serve well, you will be taught. 

Whether you can open God's storehouse and draw out God's love or not determines whether you become the Lord or not. 

A person with a family who does not feel their family and children as enemies while walking the path of the will cannot be called a true saint. A woman must feel God's love as a wife, mother, and daughter, and a man must feel God's love as a husband, father, and son. Therefore, one must evangelize. 

The headquarters church is connected to 120 holy sites in 40 countries around the world as a central holy site. Korea, despite having a 5,000-year history, has not been able to secure a sovereign status, so ultimately, it seeks to establish a heavenly sovereignty that can be assured. 

The universe is the embodiment of God's sincerity. 

Unification Church members must abandon selfishness. Married couples should receive blessings only after reaching a point where they can forget each other's bodies. In the future, blessings can only be given to those who are spiritually guided. 

Before God, an individual must remain celibate for 70 years. However, due to the emergence of the Unification Church, the 70 years have been reduced to 7 years, and further to 7 months. The period from 1960 to 1967 is the period of the great tribulation of 7 years. Jesus had to walk the seven-year course from the age of 33. 

Living with sincerity and being immersed in sincerity is the fulfillment of life. The place of sincerity is the place of acquisition. 

The period of using the flesh is like a dream. However, the tasks to be done during this period are serious. It is serious, which is why it is exhausting and tiring. 

To put forth sincerity for the teacher, one must first have a record of having put forth sincerity for the teacher's beloved nation and humanity before putting forth sincerity. 

8)
The Age of Prosperity 
The age of prosperity, this is a good word. Everyone likes the term age of prosperity. 

Then, if there is someone who created all things, would that person like the term age of prosperity, which everyone likes, or dislike it? Both the foolish and the wise like it, and all people like it, so surely the one who created humans would also like it. 

What is the age of prosperity that everyone desires? Literally, it refers to a time when everything is fulfilled and prosperous. It means a time when everything is achieved and flourishes, and that is socialized, nationalized, and globalized. 

If there is joy that humans should welcome on earth, what kind of joy would that be? Simply put, it would be the joy felt upon welcoming the age of prosperity. The God who created humans must have wanted to give humanity the age of prosperity. And God Himself must have surely desired the highest age of prosperity where He could rejoice with humans. 

The higher the person, the more they want even the lowest of people, those at the very bottom, and those living in poverty to rejoice together on the day of joy. Even the most wicked dictator, if they have joy, wishes that the entire nation rejoices with them, and even their enemies would rejoice with them. 

Even a monarch who mercilessly and pitifully slaughtered enemies until yesterday would want the citizens of that nation, as well as the citizens of the enemy nation that fought against their sovereignty, to rejoice when they meet the day of victory. No matter how cruel a dictator may be, they cannot help but wish for that. 

If that were the case, that monarch would have achieved a great victory in the midst of victory. If they created an environment where everyone could rejoice, they could truly be called a victor who can move history and create the world. 

However, historically, when one side rises, the other side tends to fall. When viewed in terms of nation against nation, they have always clashed and developed. They have developed from small to large, from nation to world. 

Thus, there are those who have a time of victory and welcome the age of prosperity, while conversely, there are those who suffer from defeat. At such times, the sorrowful side, which is in the opposite position of the victorious side, has never welcomed or longed for the victorious side. 

Here, we can identify that the highest joy that humans conceive or the praise of glory upon welcoming the age of prosperity is ultimately limited and cannot transcend borders to become global. History has developed like this. 

There is a Korean proverb that says, "When a cousin buys a field, it makes you feel bitter." A cousin is a very close brother when viewed from the perspective of a father, and they are of the same root when viewed from the perspective of a grandfather. Yet, even among brothers within three generations, if one person does a little better, they twist their mouths. This is the nature and essence of fallen humans. 

However, any sovereign wishes for even enemy nations to rejoice with them when they have glory. Here, we must understand that the wishes of a sovereign nation and the individual wishes that manifest in a one-to-one living environment do not correspond. The sovereign wishes for even enemies to praise their joy. Therefore, when a brother does well, they should rejoice, but instead, they dislike it. Isn't this strange? From this perspective, you must understand that the circumstances of a sovereign responsible for a nation and the circumstances of an individual are different. 

National Fate and Heavenly Fate 
Then, why must a person in the position of a leader who is responsible for guiding the fate of a nation hold hopes that differ from their personal circumstances? It is not because they want to do so, but because if they do not, they will be placed against the historical direction. Looking at history so far, we can see that even if one has enjoyed great glory for a time with such an environment, that glory does not last long. 

You must keep in mind that the standard for an individual to advance and the standard for a nation to advance on behalf of history are different. 

A person who governs and is responsible for leading a nation does not bear the responsibility of an individual. Their fate is tied to the fate of the nation. Just as humans have ages and lifestyle forms that suit their physiology, nations also have ages. A nation must have physiological standards that can contribute to society. It is simply larger, but it is the same as an individual.
But what is the difference between the nation and the individual? The individual can follow the nation, but the nation must not follow the individual. The emotions or private commands of individuals are always in conflict with one another in trivial matters. However, the desires of the sovereign who leads the nation pursue a different aspect than those of the individual. When we look at this, what is the difference between the position of the individual and that of the nation? The nation follows the heavenly fortune.

The formation and development of a nation is not solely for the benefit of that nation. It carries the responsibility of organizing the world. Therefore, the nation must have another desire toward the ideology of world organization, and it must transcend the realistic position. In light of this, we must recognize that there is a heavenly fortune beyond the national fortune.

So how does heavenly fortune move? If today there is a monarch who governs a prosperous nation and enjoys glory and pleasure, does heavenly fortune follow the will of that monarch? No. Whether a sovereign or a dictator, no matter how much authority they boast, they can govern the national fortune but cannot govern heavenly fortune. We must follow heavenly fortune.

The path of heavenly fortune encompasses even enemies. Therefore, sovereigns who wish for their joy to be praised by the people of enemy nations must keep in mind that they are looking for a connection to heavenly fortune.

The internal and external prosperous eras must correspond to each other.
Another interesting point is that in a prosperous era, there must be both an external prosperous era and an internal prosperous era. A person has both a body and a mind. Just because there is a body does not mean the body and mind are one. They may seem the same, but they are not.

For example, if we consider a person named Kim, Kim has a body and a mind. Vaguely, Kim's physical form might seem to be Kim, but that is not the case. Also, it may seem that his mind is inside his body, but that is not necessarily true. Suppose Kim is greedy and disliked by many people in his neighborhood. If someone says to him, "You are such a person," his mind would not agree with that. No matter how wicked a murderer or robber he may be, his mind does not want to join the ranks of murderers. That is why he feels pain. To feel pain means he does not wish to join that rank.

When we look at people like Kim or Park, we can see that the body and mind are different. What the body likes and what the mind likes are different. In other words, the prosperous era of the body and the prosperous era of the mind must correspond, but they are opposed. This is something you all know well because you have a conscience. The prosperous era of the body and the prosperous era of the mind are different.

What is corruption? It is when the mind and body are not in their rightful places. When the absolute God created humans and equipped them with the reality to appear boldly before the universe as intended, that person is one who has a place where the mind and body can stand together. If such a person exists, all environments will move according to that person's rhythm. Not having such a place is corruption.

Therefore, the mind wants to go east while the body wants to go west. Isn't that strange? What the mind aims for and what the body aims for are different. In light of this, we cannot deny that humanity has fallen.

Humans were born unknowingly according to God's absolute purpose. Therefore, there should be physiological phenomena that align with and correspond to that purpose, yet today we cannot deny that the positions and directions of the mind and body are different.

I am me, and both my mind and body are me, but when we ask if the body is my body and the mind is my mind, one does not even know that. Originally, the body and mind should be united and inseparable, and God should not be separable either, as they must fulfill their purpose with an absolute standard.

Will the highest ideal prosperous era of life come to someone whose mind and body are in different places? It is absolutely impossible to conclude that it will come. No matter how much one strives to pursue and realize a utopian ideal, it is absolutely impossible from a standpoint where the mind and body are in different places.

Even a person with a crooked nose demands a prosperous era. A disabled person does the same. Even the disabled demand a prosperous era more than others to be able to praise them. However, it is impossible to welcome a prosperous era from a standpoint where the mind and body are separated.

So what should be done? To welcome a prosperous era, one must either strike the body to draw the mind or strike the mind to draw the body; one of these must be done. However, while one can cultivate the mind by striking the body, one cannot cultivate the body by striking the mind. You will know this well through your conscientious living. If one leans even slightly toward the body, the mind rejects it. This is not something anyone instructs; there is always a struggle between two worlds in this heart. If we do not remove the 38th parallel that divides these two worlds and achieve peace, not only will world unification be impossible, but the construction of heaven will be even more impossible.

That is why Jesus said, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." So how will we realize this kingdom of heaven that is within us? It must be manifested through the body. Ideals must be practiced and realized through the body. They must be socialized, popularized, and universally validated. Only then do they have value as ideals.

The role of a true person
So where are you going now? Everyone is at a crossroads. Whether one is talented or not, whether one is disabled or not, all humans in the world are at a crossroads. The sages of the past, including Confucius and Jesus, were the same. Today, those who boast about something are no different.

So how will we resolve this crossroads? From the individual to the world, everything is divided into two paths, and you must understand that the problem of how to unify this is a greater issue than resolving the external struggles to manage the world.

From this perspective, if the physical prosperous era and the spiritual prosperous era, the bodily prosperous era and the mental prosperous era become completely one, then a peaceful kingdom will inevitably come about. In that case, everything—the people living there, those being born, the form of the nation, the natural world, and all the phenomena that manifest—will become one.

However, humans today are all feeling conflict between the two paths of the mind and body. Today, materialists argue that the mind also changes according to the environment. The mind should always have subjectivity and govern the environment, but today humans are unable to do so.

The prosperous era of the body and the prosperous era of the mind must align. Do you think that is possible? Do you think there is a chance? It is not possible with what we currently have, which is why we have come forth.

The struggles throughout history, from the clan era to the tribal era to the national era, have not been motivated by any economic issues. You must understand that the struggle of the body and mind occurred first before any environmental struggles. The resolution of environmental struggles may be temporary, but the struggle to find peace between the body and mind is ongoing throughout history.

In the past, Confucius, Jesus, and Buddha all faced this, and even if a sage emerges in this era, the struggle between the body and mind will continue. The methods and aspects of the struggle are always between the body and mind. Until now, humanity has not been able to transcend into a new third environment. Herein lies the question of what life is. That is why someone like Paul lamented, "Oh, wretched man that I am!"

The history of this struggle has not yet ended. Even if the ideal communist world that communism speaks of is realized today, the struggle between the body and mind will continue.

So what is the fundamental problem? Resolving the external environment is an indirect issue, while the direct issue that must be resolved is the struggle between the body and mind centered on the self. How to resolve this is the fundamental problem. This struggle between the body and mind is an internal struggle and motivation, while the struggles of the world are external struggles and results. However, people in the world only know external struggles. Therefore, they try to manage the world based on the results.

If God, who created the heavens and the earth, has a plan for creating an ideal human, that world will be one where the prosperous eras of the body and mind are unified. So when will the prosperous eras of the body and mind be unified? Will this unification occur at some point in the historical era, the end times, or at the end of days? For that, we cannot rely on fake people. We need true people.

So what is true? The true does not change. The true must not change. If the highest ideal person who does not change appears throughout history and establishes a prosperous era, that prosperous era must not change. There may be differences in external environments, but there must be no differences in the internal. In other words, while there may be differences in the environment, there are no differences in the mind. The hearts of workers and kings are the same. There may be class differences, but from the standpoint of the original human heart, there should be no differences. From this perspective, even those who do not know whether God exists will come to understand the demands of the times.

We must welcome the prosperous era through heavenly fortune.
To manage the human world and achieve the highest prosperous era where all people become one is the demand of our current era, which is increasingly pursuing a unified world. However, the more such demands arise, the easier world unification does not become.

Do you think democracy or communism will work? No, it will not. You must understand that it absolutely will not work. It cannot be done. A forced unification cannot create a unified world, nor can it establish an eternal world. When a form that can unify appears, another form that opposes it will emerge. Using dialectics as an example, dialectics states that unity is achieved through struggle between opposites. However, opposition implies that the concepts are already different. Opposition is only possible when there are two concepts. These two concepts may struggle, but they do not unify; they are opposed. Plus entities push each other away. They try to separate from each other.

This is what communism institutionalizes by strengthening external oppression. They do not recognize their limitations while rising above their highest authority. That world is an unstable world.

In the human world, there are human ethics and heavenly ethics, as well as national fortune and world fortune. If one tries to move the world fortune centered on national fortune, it will lead to ruin. That is where division begins. What must America do to avoid ruin? To avoid ruin, America must save the weaker nations. To save them, it must dig into the deepest vaults of their wealth. Then America will not fall. You will understand what the teacher has said when you reflect on it.

Jesus also liked the prosperous era. The teacher also likes the prosperous era. Do you like it? If you like it more than the teacher, I will yield this prosperous era to you. However, because you like it less than the teacher, even if you dislike it, the teacher must possess it.

God likes the prosperous era more than any great person in history who has liked the prosperous era, which is why the true owner of the prosperous era is God. Even if one becomes a servant, one wants to be the servant of a famous wealthy person in that neighborhood. If one must be a servant, would one not want to be the servant of the richest family? If there are two wealthy people in that neighborhood, one good and one bad, which house would you want to serve? There is no need to ask. Everyone prefers something greater, higher, and more valuable.

If that is the case for humans, what about God? Would God prefer the very last? God desires to unify the world and welcome the highest prosperous era where the entire universe becomes one, and humans rejoice. However, there is one thing to be cautious about in this joy. It should not only be humans who rejoice, but we must also invite God to rejoice together.

If there is good news in Korea, and if there is something that can be proudly reported globally, journalists will come and report it worldwide. They will promote that anyone who is interested should rejoice together. Similarly, if the world becomes one and welcomes a prosperous era, it should not only be humans who rejoice, but we must also invite God to rejoice together. Is this a good thing or a bad thing?

Do you prefer to hear the president's direct address or a representative's address? Everyone dislikes representative addresses. When we consider this, when all the nations of the world unite and welcome a brilliant prosperous era that has never been seen in history, if humans know that God, who is the center of the universe, is present, everyone will say, "God, please come!" If there is someone at that time who says, "God, do not come," that person is a thief. Why? Because achieving a prosperous era through the unification of the world cannot be done through national fortune. It must be through heavenly fortune.

So who moves this heavenly fortune? God moves it. If we have welcomed the prosperous era by riding on the heavenly fortune that God moves, we must center our joy around that God who moves.

The teachings of religion
From this perspective, to welcome a prosperous era, we must remove the barriers between body and mind. What is being advocated to break this down? Teaching human ethics and morality centered on a general historical perspective may align with social systems, but it is merely an educational method centered on the sovereignty of a nation. That alone is not sufficient. What must emerge in the human world is something that transcends nations, transcends ethnicities, and transcends the world to align with heavenly fortune. It must manifest in the historical process. That is precisely the religion that modern intellectuals and young men and women dislike. What does the character for "religion" mean? It means "the highest peak." Where does "peak" refer to? It refers to the very top. Therefore, the teachings of religion are the highest teachings among teachings.

So who are those who dislike religion? They are the failures. Such humans are those who, like animals, merely eat and drink and disregard life, being worse than animals.

Religion continues to fight to narrow the gap between the two worlds. So who does that? Humans do, but at the very top, God is always conducting it. 

Thus, there must be a prophet who serves as a servant before God, who is at the very top of humanity. There must be someone to bridge the invisible God and visible humans, who will take on the role of connecting them.
As a prophet, many prophets have appeared throughout history. 

So what does religion teach? Does it teach us to eat, enjoy, and dance as our bodies desire? It is becoming increasingly difficult to teach the youth as time goes on. I wish the teacher could buy a plaza as big as Seoul and gather all the young men and women from across the land to have a big twist dance party. Then they would never want to dance again. There is also a limit to drinking. If one cannot gauge their capacity and continues to drink, they will end up dead from a burst stomach. 

In this way, there are limits in the age of physical prosperity. To prevent the downfall of a nation, we must awaken quickly. There are ways to stop the desire to dance and play. If we force them to dance for about three years, they will get tired of it and stop. Such strategies exist.

Good aligns with eternity, while evil aligns with the moment. Every matter has a beginning and an end. Whether good or bad, if there is a beginning, there will eventually be an end. Good things have a long history, so their end comes later, while bad things tend to end quickly. Good aligns with eternity, while evil aligns with the moment. The pleasures of downfall are enjoyed in an instant, while the pleasures of prosperity are enjoyed in eternity; thus, the foundation for pleasures that can be enjoyed eternally lies not in the body, but in the heart.

Therefore, religion yearns for the heart's friend, the heart's Lord, the heart's teacher, the heart's great king, the heart's nation, the heart's people, and the heart's world, and promotes such ideals. 

Is religion good or bad? "It is good." You answer well. How good is it? Very good, right? Religion is very important in life. Those who feel that through religion they can go on a good path are the ones who succeed in their life journey. 

What kind of power does Jesus have? Ah, because Jesus is the Son of God, would it be correct to say that he would come in first place in a marathon, or that he would always be the world champion in every field? He is a champion, but what kind of champion? He is the champion of the heart world. In the history of humanity, no one can match him in gathering the fragmented hearts. In loving God, it is better when many people love God together rather than just one person loving God alone. Similarly, you all need to love Korea more. 

Do you love the world? If you love the world, what are the conditions for that love? Would you answer that you love it just in words? It should not only be a condition but should also manifest in reality. You must do what others cannot do. 

The owner of America is someone who loves America more than anyone else, materially, spiritually, and physically. Who can be a candidate for president in Korea? It must be someone who loves Korea more than anyone else. 

Who is the owner of America? It is God. Because it is God who loved the land of America even before people settled there. Who is the owner of Korea? It is God who has loved the land of Korea since before the Korean people were established. He is the God who has loved us without change even in the hardest times. Therefore, God is the owner. That is why if you become unchanging sons and daughters of God, you can say that the land of America is my land, the land of Korea is my land, and the land of the world is my land. It is because of love that this is so. 

Do you love the world? If you love the world, you must set conditions. If there is a mother who can shed tears for the world, her son will become someone who can rule the world. What is not thought of cannot become a connection, and what is not connected cannot be realized. That is why those who are sincere are welcomed. Everything in the world is like that. Therefore, Unification Church members must love the world. You must love the world more than I do. Thus, we must welcome the age of prosperity. 

Until now, Buddhism, Confucianism, and all religions have been established under God's providence. However, they have not yet welcomed the age of prosperity based on the principles of the Way. At no time has a religion ruled the world centered on the sovereignty of a nation. The issue is how to establish an ideological standard that can overcome the age of prosperity in order to welcome the age of the Way. 

Therefore, we must cultivate an internal foundation for a new era that can establish a new history on that foundation. We must create a world where we can achieve an internal age of prosperity. If such an era is not established, the kingdom of peace will never come. 

We are looking toward such a world and moving forward with the ideology that can create that world, so we must integrate the external standards of prosperity with the internal foundation of prosperity and become one with God. Thus, at the final point of victory for all nations and all creation, we must return victory to God and reach a place where we can eternally regard Him as our Father, and only then will the restoration of all things be realized. You must clearly understand that although many ages of prosperity in history have gone through ups and downs, from that point on, an eternal age of prosperity, that is, an eternal peaceful kingdom, a heavenly kingdom on earth, and a millennium kingdom will be established. 

We Unification Church members have embarked toward that world and are still fighting to create that world.
