to overcome, they must understand that the path to the original homeland is not one of conflict or strife. It is a journey centered on love—parental love, spousal love, love for children, sibling love, and love among relatives. This is the essence of living in the original homeland.

When you seek your homeland, you must remember that your relatives were born and raised there. You carry the mission to share the principles of love alongside the natural beauty that your relatives cherish. To possess the strength of love, one must have a connection to their homeland. Thus, the homeland is a place of longing.

Those who can yearn for their homeland live with a sense of fulfillment. If that homeland is a place where all people can yearn for and where blessings can dwell, we would not seek elsewhere but would enjoy family life centered on parental and sibling love, living immersed in that love.

Throughout history, countless people have come and gone. Among them were many prophets and sages. Yet, has anyone proclaimed that this land is the true homeland where all people can eternally dwell? All the sages have passed, and the hometowns where they were born have been forgotten.

Going further back, if we were to ask Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, if they had a true homeland, they would likely respond that they did not. A homeland is a place where happiness is sung, where one is immersed in parental and familial love, governing all creation while living joyfully for eternity.

Did Adam and Eve live centered on the love of such a homeland? They did not. Who has witnessed their inability to live in such a homeland? Did they see it or not? The answer is uncertain, but they did not see it. They did not directly witness it, but they heard about it. Hearing is one thing, but seeing is another. While anyone can hear, not everyone can see.

When a radio station broadcasts, anyone can hear it, but is it better to hear or to see? Of course, seeing is better. While hearing is good, it does not satisfy completely. For example, when one is moved by music, they want to see the composer. They wish to resonate with the musical world of that composer, to feel the deep essence of their music.

So, do you know whether Adam and Eve lived in their homeland by seeing or by hearing? You should know by seeing. However, no one has seen it directly. Since the ancestors of humanity did not see their homeland, their descendants have not seen it either. Thus, the human world is a fallen world, a world of evil.

What kind of place is the original homeland? It is not a place where evil dwells; it is a world overflowing with original love, where happiness is sung eternally in a world of everlasting unity. Yet, has anyone lived in such a place? Not a single person has. Many have sought such a world throughout history, but it has not been established on this earth. Many have spoken of what that world is like, but no one has practically realized it.

The same goes for Confucius and Jesus. Jesus came to establish the original homeland, but he could not establish it before he left. He said, "The kingdom of heaven is within your heart," but he did not directly see the kingdom of heaven. Throughout the historical process, no matter how great the prophets and sages were, they did not see that one place or meet that one day, and all people who inherited the lineage of fallen ancestors have yet to connect with their homeland.

Therefore, everyone is searching for ideals. They are seeking to find their homeland. What kind of world will that be? It will not be a world of rivalry and jealousy, where one feels envious when others succeed or suffers when others are happy. The success of one person represents the success of the whole, and the joy of one person is the joy of all. Thus, when one person is happy, the whole rejoices.

Has anyone lived in such a world until now? Perhaps someone has spiritually experienced it, but no one has lived that life in reality. Hence, people continue to seek a better place, a better world, an ideal world. Those who walk the path of virtue or engage in faith must overcome the difficulties of their environment.
What is the purpose of resolutely deciding and pledging, both internally and externally, to go despite the arrows of persecution? The answer is simple: to seek a better place, a better place.

Then, how good is that place? Is it a place that meets our known standards, a place we desire? Is it a place that all humanity longs for? Is that place, based on the standards that all humanity looks towards, truly the original homeland? Is the original homeland, as we perceive it, the final destination that humanity must reach? Is it an ideal world? This is something no one knows.

Why does conscience constantly command?

Each nation in the world has different cultural backgrounds, social systems, and lifestyles, so the direction in which they envision the world of the original homeland is also different. Furthermore, the direction envisioned by our church members differs from that of people in the world. While the world may focus on the physical, we focus on the spiritual; while the world may focus on the external, we focus on the internal. In this respect, our church and their direction differ.

Even among people living within the same environmental sphere across cultures and times, the direction they aspire to is different, so their desired original homeland and destination are also different. However, the fact that all humans seek a better place is the same.

What you cannot help but experience in your daily life is that, whether in personal or social life, your heart interferes with every story you encounter throughout the 24 hours of a day. It tells you, "You shouldn't do that," "You shouldn't go there," "You should go this way," "You shouldn't let that person stay," "You should wake that person up," and so on, with conscience intervening in every detail.

If you were to ask that conscience why it interferes so, the answer would be simple: it longs for a better self and wishes for a better self to live in a better environment, which is why it commands me day and night.

Then, to what extent does conscience hope for and command something good? Would it be satisfied merely by providing a place to stay, solving the issues of food and clothing, for a poor traveler who has not a penny to his name? Even if it might feel satisfied at that moment, that satisfaction would not last a week. While it may rejoice and feel good at that moment, when looking at the entirety of one's life, conscience does not allow one to rest there. It does not say that this is a place where one can rest forever, but rather commands to go on and on.

If a teacher were a billionaire and shared enough money to benefit not only the 30 million people of South Korea but also the unborn children, would that feel good? Of course, it would. But then, if you were to ask your heart if it is now satisfied, how would it respond? Would it say, "Yes, I am completely satisfied"? Absolutely not. It would say, "Ah! Share with all 3 billion people of the world!" The heart has such tendencies.

Who has the most desires in the universe? It is God. When the teacher went to the holy land this morning and sat quietly in the garden, he noticed many small insects. The birds were chirping, and the smell of earth was wafting, making him feel that the mysteries of nature are truly wonderful. He thought, "God has created so many things with great desire." When you go to a grassy area and look closely, you can see small insects moving about. If you gently part the grass, you can find flat insects, round insects, pointed insects, and all sorts of creatures moving around.

However, unaware of this, when we sit comfortably on the grass, the little insects that were moving about cry out in despair, "Oh no, I'm going to die! Please save me!"

God, who has many desires, has creatures that, like humans, possess respiratory and digestive systems, though they may not be visible. How amazing is that? You may think that world is simple, but it is anything but simple. In the future, the teacher plans to establish a global researcher to explore such worlds.

If God had no desires, would He have created such things? The God who created this world has infinite desires. Because such a God sent Jesus to this earth, Jesus also had infinite desires. Therefore, Jesus sought to give infinitely to this world. Because God has many desires, the teacher also has many desires.

When looking at the ocean, there are all kinds of fish living there. The earth is also vast, isn't it? After traveling to many countries, the teacher found it fascinating that various races inhabit this planet. Compared to such a planet, how big is the sun? The sun is 1.3 million times larger than the earth, so just imagine how immense it is.

Many planets come together to form the solar system, and these planets do not move randomly. Centered around the sun, some planets revolve a few times a year, while others revolve a few times in ten years, a hundred years, or even a thousand years, all without colliding or drifting away from their positions.

In comparison, the lives of people living on this earth are like children's games. In fact, they are even less than that, as insignificant as a speck of dust. Yet, those who cling to this tiny existence claim to be the crown of creation. How pitiful is that? When children ride on the small airplanes in the park, they get dizzy after just a few rounds and shout, "Hey! Hey!" Now, imagine the people who cling to the earth, which spins once every 24 hours. How ridiculous is that? Yet, they still proclaim themselves as the crown of creation. How pitiful they are!

Only humans possess such qualities and desires among all beings. Only humans, who wish to live forever among the myriad of creations in the universe, have such desires. If we were to unfold the human heart, how vast would it be? It would not be filled even if we gathered all of South Korea and the entire universe. The human heart has the capacity to embrace even the most desire-filled God.

Because humans possess this noble heart, they are called the crown of creation. If humans did not have such a heart, they would be miserable. They are miserable because they do not know who their Father, God, is.

Humans are precious beings because they possess such a heart. So, what does this heart command? It commands not to enter the realm of evil, even if it means death. Evil is destined to perish, while good, no matter how much it is persecuted, will not perish and will ultimately triumph.

All the saints and sages throughout history have walked the path that, from a worldly perspective, leads to ruin. However, the historical and global fortunes that guide an era can be influenced, but they cannot block the path of heavenly fortune. Those who work within the realm of heavenly fortune can transcend worldly and historical fortunes. The global fortunes that can move the world also operate within the goal of the God who created heaven and earth.

The end of human desire

Everyone, isn't the weather nice today? While the weather in South Korea is pleasant, if we look at the weather around the world, there are places with typhoons, places where tsunamis are raging, places where it rains, and places where it snows. All sorts of phenomena occur in different places. However, these phenomena occur within the earth's atmosphere.

Now, looking beyond this small planet to the vast universe, what kinds of phenomena are happening there? There are events occurring that we cannot even imagine, unfolding in absolute and mysterious harmony in countless forms.

That is why our hearts desire something better. Even if we were to gather all the wealth of the 30 million people of South Korea and fulfill our wishes, our hearts would still have desires. How much does the heart desire? Even if it were to conquer God, it would still feel insufficient and demand more. It would say, "Do more, do more." Even conquering God does not bring rest.

Then, what must the heart seek in order to finally obtain eternal stability and rest? It cannot find rest by conquering enemies, nor by conquering Jesus, nor by conquering God, who created the universe. However, that does not mean the heart moves without purpose.

Nothing acts without purpose. If you observe chemically, you will understand well that no molecule moves without purpose. It will never act in a way that is detrimental to itself. The law of heaven and earth is that they move to be beneficial to each other.

If we cannot deny that our conscience acts, does that conscience act without purpose? If not, what is the purpose of the conscience's action? The ultimate point of that purpose lies with God, not with oneself. In other words, humans must conquer the unfallen love that resides within God to be considered successful. You must understand this clearly.

The one God, to conquer all of God's love and to set aside one's own duties to resolve the grievances of history and find rest, will cause God to dance and the world to dance as well. The heart dreams of such a day. Isn't that wonderful?

The ultimate purpose of walking the path of virtue is not to go to heaven or to know God. It is to conquer God's love.

The desire to go to the most beautiful and highest eternal world is inherent in humans. This instinct resembles whom? It resembles God. The desire of the Heavenly Father exists, and because humans are created as the sons and daughters of that Heavenly Father, their instincts are shaped by that standard.

Therefore, the human heart desires to eternally unite with God and to touch the standards of true human life, wishing to live with a true heart. When the center of the true heart is established, the desire of humans is to eternally graft onto true love.

God and humans are Father and Son.

Until now, there have been many religions worldwide, but what should these religions teach? All religions must first teach about God. A religion that does not teach about God is not a religion. A religion that teaches about God in a vague manner is an uncertain religion.

So, what kind of religion is a true religion? A true religion is one that teaches who God is, what His character is like, and what His love is like. Among the world's religions, if there is one that has such deep internal significance, it is Christianity.

How has Christianity taught about God? It has taught that He is a Father. That is why we call Him God the Father. The people on earth must receive the Lord, who comes in the same position as the Father, as the Bridegroom. And the bride who will receive that Bridegroom is the believers in God. In this way, Christianity has proclaimed the standard that becomes the center of every family. Why is that?

The places that many religious seekers aim for are those where the heart can dwell forever. If there is truth in their religions, that truth must be able to teach about God clearly. It must also be able to teach about the relationship between God and humans. Furthermore, if love is not the center of that teaching, it is nothing but a rumor. The differences in the doctrines taught lead to the divisions among religions.

Among the numerous religions, centered around Christianity, Jesus declared, "I am the only begotten Son of God. No one else has been born as the Son of God in the human world." To be born as the Son of the Father means to have received the essence and blood of the Father. It means that the blood of God the Father flows within Him, that His flesh is intertwined with the Father, and that His bones are connected with the Father.

The relationship between parents and children is such that when the child is sad, the parent becomes even sadder, and when the child is happy, the parent becomes even happier. Such a bond between father and son cannot be severed by any official or legal means, nor can it be denied by any power or honor. Is that not so? Even if someone were to appear and threaten you with a knife, demanding that you deny your father, you might verbally deny him to escape that situation, but deep down, you would affirm, "He is my father. I am his child." No one can deny this. Even someone with the intellect to revolutionize the universe cannot deny this. There is no basis anywhere to deny the bond between father and son.

From this perspective, we must understand that when Jesus called God His Father on this earth, He was proclaiming to all creation that He came with the privileged central mission to govern all generations.

The purpose of Christianity

In the process of seeking God the Father, you are in the position of bride and bridegroom. Therefore, Christianity is the religion of the bride. It is a religion that must introduce to the human world the deep love that is embedded in the very marrow of the Father. While many religions have discussed truth as freedom or ideal concepts, Christianity is the only religion that has gone through a history of struggle intertwined with love on the stage of life.

In the process of seeking the bride, Jesus is the Bridegroom, but after the wedding feast, He becomes a brother. He becomes an older brother to men and a younger brother to women.

When we say "brother," a master-servant relationship is already established. He comes in a horizontal position to establish that master-servant relationship.

A religion that only fantasizes about a three-dimensional world is not an ideal religion. A religion that has the content of a three-dimensional world and is based on the realities of a horizontal, two-dimensional world cannot be an ideal religion. This is because humans are made of heart and body; the heart must relate to the three-dimensional world while the body must relate to the two-dimensional world to establish an ideal foundation in both worlds. That is the world of love. Therefore, after meeting Jesus, we become brothers and sisters.

Would you prefer Jesus to be your Lord, or your brother, or older brother? The relationship of bride and bridegroom is always precarious. A couple can divorce at any time. But can the relationship between siblings be severed? No matter how hard one tries to cut it, they cannot sever the bond of blood. That is why the relationship between siblings is better.

What has Christianity sought until now? What has Christianity longed for? It is to serve God, to serve the Bridegroom sent by God, and to prepare a bride to welcome that Bridegroom. It is also to seek out those children and to prepare a lineage with whom they can enjoy together.
Yes, it is about organizing a nation that can restore the world together with that race and forming a unified world state with them. The purpose of many religions trying to evangelize more is also there. It is to unite the world centered around the Way. Therefore, all religions in the world aim to create a chosen people through evangelism, and then to make the world one hometown, with all people as relatives and as God's people. In this, our Korean nation is the lineage. We are the descendants who believe in the religion. We are also the chosen ones. Even so, we must unite with Westerners, that is, with both white and black people. What unites us is love. That love must be a love that flows together with God's blood and flesh. All people live in different environments, but in terms of being human, whether white or black, it is the same. If a person marries a black woman and has black children, and then marries a white woman and has white children, that person becomes both a black father and a white father. In other words, their fathers are one father. Unless we cultivate a feeling that all humanity is born of one father and is one brother, the unification of the world is impossible, and the gathering of generations is impossible.

When we look at the young men and women of the world, even if they love someone, if someone better appears, they change their hearts and love that person. Also, when a partner appears who meets all conditions and is respected by the world, they want to love that person more than the one they have liked until now. This is the nature of human desire. Perhaps husbands in the world would be displeased if their wives believe in Jesus. Because their wives come to love Jesus more than their husbands. The same goes for looking at Jesus and God. Would Jesus say, "Do not love God, but pray for me"? We must love God, the Father, more than Jesus, the bridegroom.

When we connect to God's love, when asked whether the bridegroom is better or the children are better, the children are better than the bridegroom. Couples can separate, but they cannot separate from their children. Even if they are cut off from the family tree, they cannot separate because they share blood. A bride and groom can forget each other after divorce, but as time passes, they miss and long for their children more and more. Anyone who has had children knows this well. Even parents living in the world of Satan cannot deny this. That is why God loves His children.

So, who do we hope Jesus will be? We hope He will be our bridegroom. We also hope He will be our Father. Therefore, we must step beyond the love of the bridegroom and seek the love of the Father, God's love. Jesus did not come to introduce only His love, but to enable all people to receive God's love through His love. That is why Romans 8:39 states, "Neither height nor depth, nor any other creature shall be able to separate us from the love of God, which is in Christ Jesus our Lord." No one can separate us from God's love that is in Christ Jesus. However, it is possible to separate God's love from the love of Jesus alone. Therefore, the ultimate goal is to receive God's love.

Do Unification Church members like to be loved or not? People in the world say that the Unification Church dances naked and makes all sorts of accusations, but to be honest, I have never danced even once. Yet I have heard such things. Don't you want to be loved? Of course, Unification Church members also want to receive God's love. But have you seen God? Have you seen His heart? Although we cannot see God or His heart, He certainly exists. He is indispensable. If someone were to say to a person, "You are a person without a heart," would that person feel good? A person without a heart is a dead body.

The purpose of all things in the universe is to act. The human heart moves. You all know well from the Principle of Creation that when the subject and object become mutual standards and give and receive well, power is generated. When power is generated, they become one, and when they become one, they reproduce. The subject cannot act alone. Liking someone is the same; it is the mutual power that acts. To like someone means that my heart and that person's heart resonate. When you come to like someone, your heart moves back and forth for no reason. That heart is so strong that it pulls your body, making you feel like you would die without that person. This is how what the world calls fate acts.

Good people like good people, and bad people like bad people. Everything in the world is like that. For example, when playing sports, good runners gather to run, and in wrestling, good wrestlers gather to wrestle. Similarly, our hearts do not just move randomly. The subject and object must act in some way. And that action is not done to incur loss. Think about it. Who would want to like someone to incur a loss? No one does business to incur a loss. Likewise, our hearts do not move to incur a loss. The reason I am speaking to you now is not to incur a loss but to leave some benefit. In this way, all beings act to gain something without incurring a loss; this is all part of God's providential action.

No one does anything to incur a loss. If you look closely at children's behavior, you will see this. How would children know to act that way? Animals are the same. Animals also move for their own benefit. If you go out to Myeongdong and stop people passing by to ask, "How much have you lost today?" the person being asked would feel very uncomfortable. Even if you ask someone who has not incurred a loss, they would feel bad, but if you ask someone who has actually incurred a loss, they might say, "Well, I lost today," but they would still be upset. This is because everyone dislikes admitting they have incurred a loss, even if they have.

Then what is the fundamental purpose of such actions? It is to add. Everything acts to add. All actions are for the sake of gaining benefits, not for incurring losses.

Everything is equal. Therefore, the foundation is peace and harmony, loyalty and harmony. Equality can be said to be horizontal, but horizontality does not just happen. There must be some action through which the upper and lower relationships, the high and low relationships, become horizontal. Because there is a high and low, there must be an action that receives from the high and adds to the low to become horizontal.

Now, when we look at humanity, is it horizontal? No, it is not. Humanity is in a low position. Therefore, it must receive from a high place to achieve horizontality. That is why humanity must seek a higher ideology and have a refuge for a higher spirit. This is why a higher global religion capable of leading the 20th century must emerge.

Horizontality does not just happen. It must receive power from elsewhere. Since it cannot receive power from within itself, there must be a place that provides that power. That place is a high place. It must be a good place, not a bad one. It is a place where all people want to go and live, in other words, a place where all people have ideals. So what is that ideal? It is not about eating well or sleeping well; it is true love.

The ideal of humanity is achieved through love. When you visit a close friend's house, even if you have to wear their clothes, you do not dislike it, right? Your heart and body do not shrink; even your cells become comfortable. That is why you long for your parents' embrace. However, after a while, what happens? The comfortable heart begins to feel a bit constricted. Then, in a state where you cannot do this or that, you inevitably return to your own home. Is this peace? Is this harmony? Peace means everything is resolved. Rest is the same. To untie all knots is to find rest.

Until now, humans have never experienced rest centered on their original hearts, longing for the people their original hearts desire, even for a single day in the historical process. That is why life is called a vale of tears.

In light of this, humanity must find a standard. Thus, we must love. However, love cannot be between just two people. It cannot be just between a father and his children. For people to love each other, there must be a gathering of people, and singing and dancing are necessary.

You might think that just saying "I love you" is enough, but to express love with emotion, singing is necessary. You might wonder why we need to dance when we could just stand still, but dancing is also necessary.

When a person is intoxicated by something good and sings even a little, their bones become loose, their cells stir, their eyes become misty, and tears may flow; such agitation occurs.

So why are these things necessary? Isn't it good for a father and child to just look at each other? That is love, but it is not enough. There must be a harmony of heaven and earth in that place. For that, there cannot be just God and me, or just a father and child. There must be many accompanying conditions.

If there is a father, there must be a mother; if there is a man, there must be a woman. If there were only women in the world, women would dislike only meeting women. If men lived only with men, they would feel the same. That is why if there is a father, there must be a mother; if there are parents, there must be children; and then there must be siblings.

So, for whom should I exist? For my parents? For my siblings? Who am I really for? I exist for myself. My father and mother exist for me, my siblings exist for me, and everyone exists for me. When you think this way, your mouth opens naturally with joy.

How many desires do humans have? There are people who want to take God's love and keep it all to themselves without giving it to anyone else, but if someone says they were born for their father or for their teacher, how would that make them feel? Our ancestors have come and gone for thousands of years, and they all came for me. So how important am I? That is why Jesus said, "For what shall it profit a man, if he shall gain the whole world, and lose his own soul?" (Mark 8:36).

Then who is God for? He is not a God for Himself; He is a God for me, which is the desire of humanity. When I take care of the children at home, if I first hold the older child in my arms, the younger sibling looks at me and says, "Daddy, hold me too." They gaze at the arm holding their older sibling with their little eyes and say, "Daddy, hold me too." In seeing this, we can understand that the essence of love that longs for the homeland is like that.

So, believing in Jesus is for whom? Is it for God or for Jesus? No, it is for me; I believe because of me. Then who do we believe in when we believe in the World Christian Unification Spiritual Association? It is also for me. The world I must achieve is the original world, and that original world must be achieved anyway, but how hard would it be to try to achieve that world alone?

However, if all the people belonging to that organization join forces, they can achieve that world. Yet, if I think that Jesus came to the world because of me, that God is within me, and that the world depends on me, believing that only the chosen one is me is a great mistake. As I am the subject, when the subject and object give and receive well, they become completely one. So when we stand in a place of oneness, he is me, and I am him. This is the conclusion reached through the law of love.

The world that discusses and interrogates the order of conditions to find the Way is an unstable world. Standing in a position where the order of giving and receiving is completely united around love, when you look around you, it may seem that there is no one but yourself, but you must always remember that there is a subject.

To find the homeland, what do the countless people around the world seek? They seek the land of their homeland. To do this, they must offer sacrifices. The offerings that Cain and Abel made before God in the past were also to seek the homeland. Noah spent 120 years building the ark for the same purpose: to seek the homeland. The ark was a conditional object needed on the way to find the homeland. They had to do whatever it took to shorten the path to the homeland. Abraham was the same. To find the ultimate destination of humanity, the land of the homeland, one must abandon their hometown and their country. Since the homeland cannot be two, one must also abandon the ideal world they were looking at.

To go toward the land of the homeland where all people can find rest, one must abandon their individuality, their small nation, and all their dreams. If one tries to establish a lineage centered on their dreams, it is impossible to seek the homeland. Therefore, after abandoning everything, one must wholeheartedly seek the land of the homeland. Moreover, one must live with the single-minded determination to find the true place, eating with that determination, sleeping with that determination, and experiencing joy and sorrow with that determination.

For this reason, Abraham abandoned his hometown of Ur of the Chaldeans, and Moses also abandoned the luxurious palace of Pharaoh and the position of prince to find the welfare of his people's homeland, to prepare the foundation where all people could dwell. The Israelites wandered in the wilderness for 40 years to find their homeland, and for thousands of years, they have wandered the world without a nation, also in search of the land of hope.

The countless nations scattered across the world have moved or revolted, and history has changed for the same reason: to find the land of the homeland and to go to the world of the homeland. This is the common path of destiny that all humanity must take, which is why everyone inevitably walks this path of destiny.
Who are the protagonists that must solve these issues? On this path, God is with us, and therefore, leaders who take responsibility for the way of the truth centered on God and those who follow the way of the truth must bear such responsibilities. They have the mission to prepare the homeland on a global scale. For this reason, those who cannot purify the world as believers are merely humanistic religious people.

A person can only form a single personality when the heart and body are united. This personality cannot be manifested solely through the body itself. For the personality to be expressed, the body must respond through the heart. Therefore, personality manifests through human relationships in a flat environment centered on sociality.

Religion teaches about the inner realm, that is, the world of ideas, but a social practice venue is needed to implement it. Until now, religion has pursued the spiritual aspect, that is, the afterlife, but people live in the present before going to the afterlife. It is through the reality of this world that one enters the afterlife.

However, until now, religion has depicted the external world through the internal world, and the reason for this is that the external world has been corrupted. The external world has already been occupied by Satan, so it has sought the external world after preparing the internal world first. Therefore, you must understand that all humanity is destined to seek the homeland.

Many prophets and sages throughout history did not hesitate to walk the path of death to find the homeland. They died truly. There are many prophets and sages who faced martyrdom while seeking the homeland, disregarding all kinds of hardships and the path of death.

The Responsibility of Believers
You cannot go to the homeland alone. You must go through historical connections. For this reason, we humans carry historical connections. If there are achievements of your ancestors, you want to boast about your ancestors, and if there are achievements of your parents, you want to boast about your parents. If your parents have a good name, you want to say whose son you are. This means that we respect historical connections.

Today exists to prepare for tomorrow and to illuminate yesterday. Therefore, we must stand in a position that acknowledges the facts of the past, not in a position that denies them.

What can genuinely acknowledge the past in the historical journey? In searching for this, we find the true path, and in finding the true path, we find the true religion. And to introduce the homeland on the foundation of true religion, love must be included. From this perspective, Christianity holds a very important position.

So where is the mission of Christianity? It is to regard believers as life, to love one another, to be harmonious through love, and to spread love. Furthermore, that love is the source of all life.

Then, what position should those who believe in Christianity take? They must stand in a position that influences the search for the homeland of love. They must live their faith from such a position. Looking at this, peace can only be achieved through love, and all people can only be equal through love. This means that love is indispensable.

What kinds of love are there? There is internal love and external love, that is, love for the spirit and love for the material. People can also be distinguished as internal and external beings. This is true for anyone of any race.

Then, to what extent should we love? First of all, to be someone who can love, we must first stand in a position to receive God's love. To do this, we must love all people from the standpoint that God loves them. Just as God loves all people as brothers and as children, we must also stand in the position of that Father. This is why the Unification Church speaks of having the heart of a parent.

To have the heart of a parent, we must understand what the heart of a parent is, and to find the heart of a parent, we must go to the homeland. It cannot be found elsewhere. Today, many people living on this earth must go to the homeland to find the heart of their parents. No matter how much one pursues the truth or is skilled and knowledgeable in worldly affairs, one cannot become a child without passing through the heart of a parent.

A person is born through the love of their parents. We are born through the love of our parents, but we were born through the love of false parents. This means that we were not born through the love of normal parents centered on the principles of the homeland. We fell while seeking the homeland. We should have been born centered on the love of parents after entering and resting in the homeland, but we could not do that. Therefore, we must go to the homeland to find the love of our parents. You must understand that life is such that we must seek the homeland to find the love of our parents.

To become the sons and daughters of the homeland, one must be resurrected and reborn.
So how far has love fallen due to the fall? It has gradually fallen from the love of parents to the love of children, the love of siblings, the love of relatives, the love of friends, and down to the love of servants and the love of servants' servants. Therefore, to find the love of parents and walk the path to the homeland, we must go back up again. Thus, we must enter the position of the servant's servant centered on God through the life of the truth.

A servant has a master, but a servant's servant has no master. We must rise from the position of a servant's servant through the process of being a servant to the position of an adopted child. When we say adopted child, it may not feel good, right? If you have no direct descendants and must leave all your inheritance to an adopted child, would that feel good? An adopted child and a direct descendant not only differ in bloodline but also in all physical characteristics. We must rise to that position of an adopted child and receive grafting from direct descendants.

Also, when viewed from the perspective of love, we must rise from the love of a servant's servant to the love of a servant, the love of an adopted child, and the love of a direct child, and then to the love of a spouse and the love of a parent. Then, through the love of parents, we must be resurrected as children. This is what is meant by being born again in Christianity.

To pass through the heart of a parent, what must be done? A person's life must be born through the love of their parents, so there must be a standard that they have received the love of their parents to pass through the heart of a parent. Then, what love is centered on? The true owner of true love is God, so without going through the process of true parental heart and true parental love centered on God, one cannot be reborn or resurrected.

Then, when viewed from the perspective of love, what kind of person should you seek? Generally, you are longing only for the love of the other. But that alone is not enough. You must go beyond that and be resurrected and reborn centered on the heart of a parent to finally occupy the homeland.

Simply receiving the love of parents is not enough. You must be reborn centered on that love to become the sons and daughters of the homeland. Without being reborn, we cannot go to the homeland. In other words, we may reach paradise, but we cannot enter heaven.

Then, to be reborn, who must be there? Parents must be there. To save your life, you must go through a position like spending ten months in your mother's womb. Just as the fetus grows by receiving all the nutrients from the mother, you must also grow. However, we in the Unification Church are losing that position.

Simply meeting parents and receiving their love does not mean being reborn. Because you are people found from a fallen world, you must overcome the same hurdles that your parents faced in their fall. If you do not do that, you cannot enter the homeland forever. Here, a process of rebirth must occur where you once again enter the mother's womb and come out. You must grow from a position like that of a pure and innocent child. To be reborn, you must first stand in the position of entering the father's bones before entering the mother's womb. This is what the Unification Church did until 1960. That is why when you see members of the Unification Church, they feel emotionally different.

Blessing and Conditions for Restoration
No matter how much one claims to be someone seeking the homeland, they must meet the other at the level of completion. However, you are still far from reaching the level of completion. Because of the fall, you started from below the level of rebirth, not from the level of completion. Therefore, no matter how well you believe and how well you practice your faith, you must rise from the level of rebirth.

So how do we connect to the level of completion? In the life of the world, one may fall and then rise again, but on our path, once you fall, you cannot rise again. No matter how well you believe and how loud you proclaim, you must overcome the peak of completion. Without doing so, you cannot settle and live in the homeland. To enter that homeland, a life form must be resurrected based on the heart of the parents. For this, the heart of the parents must be the center; it cannot be centered on oneself.

When looking at the so-called blessing of the Unification Church, what is the issue? The issue is establishing conditions for restoration to receive the blessing. There is a profound content associated with this. Historically, you have inherited the bloodline of the fall. Therefore, to receive the blessing, you need a heavenly condition that can strike the bloodline of the fall and resolve the fundamental issues.

Thus, the Unification Church has faced persecution and has walked the path of the cross emotionally. Therefore, when you enter the Unification Church, you separate from all past personal connections. You completely sever all ties.

Since the place we must go is the homeland, we must seek the homeland. We must find the true homeland. To find the true homeland, what must we fallen people do? We must rise to the position before Adam and Eve fell. However, humanity has not yet fully restored the position before the fall.

Originally, if humans had not fallen, they would have completed the three stages of growth and lived there, but due to the fall, they could not. In other words, humans were not born through the true parental love that God could approve of and did not inherit the true parental bloodline.

Today, Unification Church members must achieve global victory and be recognized worldwide. Centered on God's heart, they must love all humanity as their own kin and walk the path of restoration. Moreover, they must advance for the sake of the nation and people or to build the heavenly kingdom on earth.

The Truth of Grafting in Christianity
At the end of days, Christianity says that the Lord will come. If the Lord comes, will He come as a man or a woman? "He will come as a man." The Lord must come as a man. Until now, everyone has been born, but they have been born as mere shadows. For example, they should have been born as toads, but they were born as frogs. They should have been born as peacocks, but they were born as roosters. That is the situation. The seed has changed.

Therefore, one must deny everything about oneself and be newly grafted. Because the types are similar, grafting can occur. In this regard, the truth of grafting in Christianity is the true truth. To graft, one must completely cut off everything from the past and bring in new purity for grafting. Thus, one must create a center that maintains their entire life by grafting in new thoughts, new vitality, and new tribes. For this reason, until now, Christianity has had to play such a role as a religion that serves.

Then, what should individual humans do? The Lord, who comes as a bridegroom, is the father of humanity. And the bride is the mother. Heaven symbolizes the man, and the earth symbolizes the woman, so the woman must come forth on the earth. Thus, the woman is called the field, and the man is called heaven. Therefore, we Unification Church members must return to the seed of life. We must return to the seed of life itself.

The Unification Church was in such a period until 1960. At that time, Unification Church members were clamoring to see the Teacher. Before the Teacher shed tears for you, you must first shed tears for the Teacher. Such things must happen. Thus, we must establish a connection with the sons and daughters who will be born from the depths of the Father’s bones, who have not yet propagated good and evil. This connection must be established centered on heart and love.

This is why when you enter the Unification Church, it feels like home. Although it is your first time, it does not feel like your first time. After receiving grace here for about three days and returning to your home, it feels like your home is a goblin house. Your husband looks like a thief, and your children look like the offspring of thieves. Strangely, it actually becomes like that. However, when you come to church, even those who seem to have no proper demeanor feel good. This is the same as anyone being good if they are from your hometown. But at home, even though they are your beloved sons and daughters, the way you treat them changes completely from before. Such changes occur, leading to a historical reversal.

Therefore, you must dive into the Lord centered on heart, so that your living emotions are the same as the Lord's, that you die as the Lord dies, that you live as the Lord lives, and that you can rejoice as the Lord rejoices. Thus, you must stand in the position of a father who has not yet married, that is, in the position of a son within the Lord. Therefore, when the Lord, who comes as a bridegroom, receives the bride and forms a couple, you must stand in a position like being reborn through that bride, that is, the mother. The period of going through the mother is the period of labor centered on the earth, which symbolizes the woman. Through that mother, you must resurrect yourself and simultaneously resurrect your ancestors and even the nation and people. Do you understand?

In this way, only through the Lord can you become someone who can live in the homeland. Only by becoming such a person can you finally call your parents "Father" and "Mother" in front of history, and you can call those who stand in such a position "brothers."

These brothers gather to form relatives, these relatives gather to form tribes, these tribes unite to form nations, and these nations come together to finally unify the world. Thus, the world must take shape centered on God and centered on God's love, forming a world that arises from one root of love. Only then will the world become a world centered on God, and the land centered on God, that is, the heavenly kingdom on earth will be established. This is the homeland where we can live forever.

The Awareness that Everything Exists for Me
Today
What is the purpose of my existence? We were born to freely serve God in a place where we have transcended all the stories of this fallen world, achieving personal resurrection along with familial resurrection, national resurrection, and global resurrection. We have entered the Unification Church bearing such a heavenly mission, and each of us must faithfully take responsibility for that mission.

Then, for whom do we take on that responsibility? Centered on God's love, did we do it for anyone else? It is for myself. The True Parents come for me, the love of the True Parents is realized for me, and even the siblings and relatives born centered on the love of the True Parents are all for me.

From this perspective, regardless of whether they are esteemed or not, relatives and tribes connected by blood must feel that their shame is my shame and their disgrace is my disgrace. Only then can one qualify to stand in place of the original person, representing the entire universe.

Therefore, my existence is cosmic, and the entirety of creation has been mobilized for the completion of just one person, and all created beings exist and move for the completion of that one person. From this viewpoint, everything you do to look at the world, praise God, and love your siblings is ultimately for me. I was born because of me, and I live for me. Loving is also for me; therefore, the more I love, the greater it becomes, the more it develops, and the deeper it gets. This love must be centered on the love of the homeland.

If there is a foolish person, think that person came because of me. So, do you all think that way? The trials that come to us Unification Church members are all for me. If you think that everything is for me, will I have enemies? There are no enemies.

That is why, even when Jesus was nailed to the cross and stabbed in the side by enemies, he did not consider them enemies but thought, "They are here to perfect me." At that moment, they may stand in the valley of my suffering, but ultimately, they are people who have come for me. Therefore, they should not be despised. If they are despised, my mission cannot be completed. With this heart, he prayed for them.

God is the same. If God thinks, "I have labored for you for 6,000 years!" then God cannot walk the path of restoration. If He thinks He has walked the path of sorrow in the 6,000 years of history because of humans, then God Himself cannot reach the homeland. Therefore, saying "because of someone" is heresy. So I must say, "I am the master. You exist because of me, and I am moving toward the ideal because of me." It is for me, not because of the Father. We must have a stronger sense of self.

The purpose of self-completion - cosmic completion
Today, we Unification Church members must surpass the remaining path of Jesus. You all know the reason well. If you do not know that, you are not a Unification Church member. You must raise your own awareness and be able to take responsibility first. The Unification Church needs such people.

When you think that everything exists for the completion of just one person, you can understand how great the human heart is. This stone, the grass on this mountain, and the trees all exist for me, and even if countless nations have different ideas and cultural backgrounds, they are all moving to fulfill my ideals. Think about how the universe revolves around just one person. When I think about the fact that I have entered that cosmic realm, it is fine to walk the path of being drawn along with God. How happy that place is where one can feel such self-worth! It is a place where one can always be thankful to God.

Whether a person has faith or not, on the surface, they seem the same as anyone else in the world. Externally, there are no signs. However, in the spirit world, it is different. The spirit world is a world similar to the earthly world. If you look at the spirit world broadly, it resembles the shape of a person. Among spirits, there are spirits like eyes, spirits like ears, and spirits like hands.

Similarly, in completing the cosmos, it is like cells gathering to form a whole. The entire cosmos is interconnected. If the blood passing through the eyes says, "Oh, I only go to the eyes and absolutely not to the toes," would that happen? No, it does not. It flows throughout the whole body, and when the time comes, it flows down to the soles. Therefore, nothing is unnecessary. Everything is necessary.

To connect with the spirits who have come and gone throughout history, we need people on earth who resemble them. That is why thirty million nations are not enough, and thirty billion people are not enough. It is because only from a position resembling those in the spirit world can a relationship be established to give and take with them. Therefore, you must know that even those who say, "Oh, I am different! I can be alone," need to be restored.

The only thing that made Jesus different from all humanity from the moment he was born is that he came as the Son of God from God. He is the Son of God. What does it mean to be the Son of God? It means to be the temple of God. Jesus exists for all people. At the same time, all people exist for me. Because he was always in this position, when he went to the cross, he did not go alone. All the ideologies centered on this universe were old, so he carried them all with him to the cross. Because of that, all beings entered the realm of the cross, but through Jesus' resurrection, they could also participate in the realm of resurrection. Therefore, one should not think, "Jesus lived alone and left; what does that have to do with us?"

From the beginning of all existence to the end of existence, everything exists for just one person.

As mentioned earlier, when viewed centered on love, everything is connected in that way. I do not love others for their sake; I love them for my sake. Each person must have that heart and go out for God so that the entire universe can unite centered on God. You must think from this perspective. Also, going beyond this standard, you must ask yourself, "What kind of person am I? I am a child of God; what should I do to fulfill God's will?" You must realize that I was born so that the universe can be completed along with my own completion.

Thus, from this position, when you pray with a heart that genuinely feels the desire to love your siblings, relatives, tribes, nations, and the world, that prayer becomes a prayer for the world.

The place where we live as God's princes and princesses is the homeland.
Before the tearful true love, the world is drawn in. The person who can bring the world into the standard of unity centered on this love can occupy the perfect homeland. However, if one cannot become such a person, they cannot go to the homeland, and even if they go to the homeland, they cannot cross over into the homeland. If one cannot enter or exit after going there, then that person has no homeland. One must become a person who can enter and exit freely. Only then can the Lord of the world dwell on this earth!

Jesus came to this earth and left by dying. He should have come freely and left freely without dying. Moreover, there should have been no persecution in doing so. Only in such a world can the kingdom of heaven be established on earth, and the world of hope that God desires can be realized, and you must understand this.

Then, the love of God that the heart desires can automatically be occupied. However, until now, there has been no son or daughter who could unite with God’s love. The person who is unified centered on God's love becomes an active subject who can govern the entire universe eternally within that realm of love, thus becoming a heavenly princess or prince. Do you understand?

God is seeking out humans through the path of restoration. That God is the Lord of all and the subject of all creation. At the same time, He is the subject of all nations. Who are the sons and daughters of God, the princes of heaven, and the princesses of heaven? The prince is the Lord, and the princess is the Lord's bride. We must be reborn centered on that Lord and bride. When that happens, the Lord and His bride become the ancestors of humanity and become parents. If we are reborn through their love, we can inherit the position of parents and stand in the position of the second prince and princess.

All people must become the sons and daughters of God. Therefore, human desire is to regard God as our Father. Even those who conquer the world and the universe long for God's love. This is true for both foolish and wise people alike. The reason why the original intention of all humanity acts to long for God's love is that there is a 100% possibility for it to be so.

Thus, the human heart has the desire to establish its original position centered on God's love because it was originally in that position. Therefore, centered on God's love, we can all occupy the positions of the princes and princesses of the heavenly kingdom. Consequently, all possessions of the heavenly kingdom and all destinies of the heavenly kingdom become ours, and the Father’s things become my things. The Father’s stories are also mine, and all the Father’s possessions are mine. When this happens, there is nothing in the world that one cannot have, and only then can one truly be happy. There, everything one needs, including love, is present, along with all the conditions beyond love. That is the place where we can finally rest, our homeland. Let us all pray.

We must long for that place with eyes that ache with longing, and we must desire that place with hearts that ache with yearning. Therefore, Father, please personally guide our hearts and bodies so that we do not become losers in this fight.

Let us feel the sorrow of the defeated deeply, and let us also feel the fact that we are fallen descendants. We must recognize anew that we exist to bring the victory and joy that the Father desires. We must respect ourselves. Without the Father’s love, we cannot find rest, and without the Father’s love, we cannot feel the Father’s heart. Please pour out waves of Your love into our lacking hearts and awaken the grace of regeneration.

Please allow us to find the land of our homeland and to find our original siblings. And please make us Your sons and daughters who can have our original parents and original children, fulfilling the joyful purpose that the Father intended to accomplish through love.

Please guide us to never act in a way that would bring loss before You. We earnestly wish and hope to be sons and daughters who can leave behind something beneficial for all. Not only in the church but also when we return home and go out into society, may we become Your sons and daughters who can fulfill the mission of pioneers and forebears by engaging in good deeds that bring joy to You, even indirectly paving the way for love.

The sorrow of all people still remains, so please allow us to pioneer a new source of life to share the gifts of love with them. We earnestly hope and wish to become contributors and forebears in establishing a foundation where You can directly operate. Please share Your love with us in the days to come, and we earnestly ask that Your eternal wishes be fulfilled through us. I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

Let us establish the reality of truth with sincerity.
<Summary of the Words> You must evangelize 12 people, three each month, during the four months from June to September. Those who oppose the Unification Church are mainly your relatives or friends, so you must pray for them and evangelize them sincerely. 

See how much heaven cooperates when you put in sincere effort. If you do not evangelize your relatives and loved ones on earth, you will not be able to escape their accusations in the afterlife. You should not speak to anyone about your sincere efforts. A believer must keep the fact of their sincerity hidden.

Originally, one enters heaven after completing the restoration of the world. Therefore, even Jesus has not yet entered heaven. This is not something that anyone can do. The one who comes as the qualified person is the Lord, and only after becoming one with Him and completing the restoration of the world can one enter heaven.

The teacher is merciless towards evil but infinitely weak towards good, which is why he fears God more than Satan. The matters of the spirit world are complex, and if one goes out with a proud attitude based only on what they have received from the spirit world, they will be broken. That is why the principle is necessary. The fall occurred because the archangel and Adam could not become one with God, so the archangel and I must unite to block Satan. This can only happen when there is an angel cooperating with me, and when I and the angel become one, I can finally block Satan.

The meaning of the restoration of indemnity
You have learned the term "restoration of indemnity." The restoration of indemnity means forgiving the greater through the lesser conditions. For example, to forgive one hundred people, if one person stands in the position of receiving punishment on behalf of those one hundred without complaint, longing only for God, possessing heaven in their heart, and enduring that position, then the sins of those one hundred will be forgiven as a result of that one good person receiving punishment.

The person standing in the position of indemnity must long for heaven even in the midst of cold and must long for God, believing that whether they die or live, it is for heaven, and that being born and living is also for heaven. One must start from heaven, go through the heavenly process, and reach the destination of heaven. By one person enduring such a position, the sins of one hundred people are forgiven. In other words, one person is set up as a representative of one hundred evil people, and by receiving punishment on behalf of the one hundred, they are restored from an evil position to a good position, which is called the restoration of indemnity. Do you understand what this means?

Then, how can we know the history of the restoration of indemnity? We can know it by observing God's providence. The history of humanity has been a history of the restoration of indemnity. How far has humanity fallen due to the fall? They have fallen to the point of not even being able to be God's servants. Originally, what were humans born as? They were born as children of God. Therefore, until they become God's body, they must grow up receiving the love of the Father. After going through the process of being like babies, they must go through the process of being sons and reach the position of oneness with God. Therefore, you must accurately know what time it is now and reflect once again on what you have done to set conditions on the path of indemnity. Do you understand? "Yes."  
As I leave for this world tour, I did not want to share such serious words with you, but I have no choice but to speak. The teacher is currently walking such a serious path. However, I do not wish for you to have a heart that simply wants to rush ahead.  
Still, it seems that the teacher loves you, right? Would you prefer that the teacher loves you or that the teacher does not love you? "It is better that you love us."  
The path of restoration is a path to be sought, and the path of principle is a path to be walked.  
The teacher and you must walk the same path, even if it means dying. Everyone you meet on the way is someone you meet due to a connection. Therefore, the teacher and you must meet that day when you can please God through this connection. We still have a path to walk.  
Once this seven-year course ends, we must again go beyond the second seven-year course. If we do not set conditions centered on the standards that must be indemnified during the seven-year course, we will have to set up the second seven-year course and go again. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That is why, as I mentioned before, you must stand in the position of Abel before twelve people, whether they are your own family or your most beloved parents, and establish a connection with them. You must do this. In other words, you must become someone who sets conditions on the path of indemnity. However, you cannot set those conditions on your own. You must follow the teacher. In other words, the path that the teacher has walked is the path you must walk.  
The struggles the teacher undergoes to love the members show you the path you must take. In the journey of faith, you must be resurrected from the world of death through the word. If you remain in that place, you will die. You must be able to feel the joy of a child who was dying being revived. There is God's value there, God's love, a value greater than my own value, and a joy greater than my own joy. Therefore, you must forget your sorrow and be able to look at that place and rejoice.  
You must feel that a single life is precious. You must become someone who can truly feel and experience the words of Jesus, "What will it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses his own soul?" (Matthew 16:26) to be qualified to govern the universe. You must be sure of this. Do you understand? "Yes."  
Are you qualified to set conditions? Are you really qualified? "I am not qualified." When have you ever loved God to the extent that you received praise from Satan, and when have you ever done something that could deeply move Satan? Because you have not done so, God has opened the path of indemnity in love for humanity and teaches you to follow until you return to the original world. That is the principle of the Unification Church.  
The path of restoration is a path to be sought, and the path of principle is a path to be walked. When the teacher came out on this path of indemnity and restoration, the teacher's entire life was a journey of seeking. So you only need to follow the path that the teacher has already found. But can you not do that? Can you not even follow? The conditions for indemnity cannot be set by someone who has not established a standard that transcends God, Satan, and the fallen realm.  
The place where indemnity takes place  
Then, since you cannot set conditions for indemnity before God and Satan, what should you do? You must rely on the teacher. Thus, you must set conditions that can lead to liberation and overcome. One must rise, and one must descend; that is, the world of Satan must descend, and the heavenly world must rise. To do that, you must become a fisherman. Therefore, you must go down. The more you try to go down, the more you will ride the fortune that rises. Indemnity does not happen in a comfortable place, a high place, or a place you desire. Do you understand?  
So where does heaven begin? It does not begin in the manger where Jesus was born. It begins from the place of Golgotha, where Jesus carried the cross. It starts from the place where life and death are judged at the crossroads of life and death, where death and resurrection, life and death intersect. Indemnity occurs in such a place. But what do we use to achieve indemnity? We do it with love.  
To the members of the Unification Church, the teacher is the master. Therefore, even if you have to give up everything in the world, you must have the heart to obey the teacher. Only then can God lead our conditions for indemnity through love. It must be a place where heaven and earth can recognize, where Satan can recognize, where God can shed tears of joy, where Satan can shed tears of sorrow, and where you can praise with joy; only there can conditions for indemnity be established and victory be achieved.  
So what does the Unification Church present? It evokes your emotional conditions. That is why the Unification Church is called the final path. The purpose is not to evoke truth. Of course, it also evokes truth and causes a revolution of character through that truth, but the main purpose is to evoke emotions.  
Cain must follow Abel. He must obey and follow the path that Abel indicates. If Abel dies, he must die, and if Abel lives, he must live. That is why you must serve the teacher with an Abel-like standard and follow the teacher with a heart that longs for Abel. This path is the final path, so you must be able to overcome even to the point of death. So far, the Unification Church is the only place that has presented such a path in the history of humanity. Do you understand? If you set conditions centered on such emotions and overcome, you can cross the final peak. Therefore, you must understand that the Unification Church is the last church.  
Only when the desires of the heart are fulfilled can God finally rest, Satan be eternally expelled from this earth, and we ourselves also find rest.  
In the end, there is only one place where such conditions can be established, and that place is the Unification Church. You must understand this. Do you understand? Yes, right? "Yes." Do you actually feel that? "Yes."  
Conditions for indemnity must be set alone  
Conditions for indemnity cannot be set by two people. Even if you have a husband, you cannot set him beside you. You cannot take your beloved parents or wife with you. Relationships in front and behind are permitted, but relationships on the left and right are not permitted. Do you understand? "Yes." If two stand together, restoration does not happen. In the world of the heart, two cannot stand. One person must be the subject.  
For the husband to stand in the position of the subject, he must absolutely obey his parents. The wife must serve her husband as if he were God. Why must it be so? Because we must achieve indemnity and restoration. The man must absolutely obey and follow the path of the husband for the relationship in front and behind to be established. Therefore, you must follow the teacher. Is that right? "Yes." When you follow, it should not be with tears and cries. You should follow with joy.  
You will not be able to forget the teacher wherever the teacher goes. Would you prefer that the teacher stays abroad for a long time or that the teacher returns quickly? "It would be better if he comes back quickly."  
What has the teacher emphasized to you until now? The teacher does not want you to gather money and live well.  
He says to establish a tradition. What kind of tradition? It is to establish a tradition of setting conditions for indemnity in the path of indemnity. You must establish such a tradition before the purpose. If you do not establish that, you will flow to other places.  
You must clearly know what position you are in now and pray and dedicate more after the teacher has started. Therefore, from now on, you must live concretely instead of vaguely as you have lived in the past. You must love your parents as you love the teacher, love your old faith companions as you love the teacher, and love this nation as you love the teacher.  
If you become like leaven and go out before the world, the world will become heaven. Do you understand? "Yes." I hope you understand this and strive to become such a person.

I earnestly hope and desire this.

Please allow the words conveyed to these people to be remembered anew. Even if others are at ease, may they become heavenly soldiers who can fight tirelessly to surpass the conditions of that rest.

I hope that you will be with us throughout the remaining days, and I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

**Responsibilities of Blessed Families**
<Summary of the Words> If one says, "Is it possible to be faithful by merely walking this path every day?" and thus prevents one from walking the path of faithfulness, that condition will become a grievance for eternity in the spirit world.

Loyal subjects and filial children are born with the national fortune, and they cannot endure without living for the purpose of the will, even unknowingly.

To fulfill Abel's responsibility, Cain must be restored. Only then can the parents be restored. In the path of faith, brothers, tribes, and nations represent Cain. Therefore, no one can restore their parents without restoring this Cain. That is why the teacher could not evangelize his own parents.

To be a filial child, one must lead the family and serve the parents. Thus, those who cannot be harmonious among siblings cannot be filial children.

The teacher originally did not like people. However, one cannot only deal with what one likes. One must also be able to treat the unpleasant well. During this period, one must fulfill the duty of filial piety. There will always be those who hinder the path of a filial child. To become the eldest son, one must embrace the siblings well in place of the parents. That is why the Bible says, "Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called the children of God." (Matthew 5:9)

There are some members who think that if I had just said a few words, they would not have been caught in the spirit world. However, that is because the time has not yet come for me to say it.

The fear of death comes because one has not accomplished all that must be done in this world. Once all is accomplished, no fear will come.

Earthly life exists for the life in the spirit world. It is like a production factory for the spirit world.
