Day of All Things
<Prayer> We thank You for establishing this day as a day we can commemorate on this earth according to the eternal purpose of Your providence. 
Father, four years ago, we designated this day before You. As we think about the historical process leading up to this day, we realize the efforts of our Father have been behind countless individuals and numerous nations. We recall once again that it was an immense history filled with grievances and indignation that we cannot even dare to imagine, and we feel that this sad history continues even now. 
Since the day the fight between Cain and Abel began, since the time when the foundation of death was established, the world of death has not been moved. And we feel that the history of our Father’s struggle has been woven together amidst humanity's inability to escape this environment. 
Now, if there are still conditions of lamentation remaining, we must resolve those conditions, and if there is still labor that we must do, we must realize that it is the labor of correcting and settling this wrong foundation. 
Our Father has always had to win from a good position. However, when we think about the fact that the environment we are in is still surrounded by sadness and pain, we long for the time when our historical ancestors and righteous predecessors fought at the forefront to establish goodness. 
The history of sorrow has arisen based on goodness, continuously emerging through hardships, only to encounter sorrow again, falling and rising again, and this history has continued. We realize that this wall of sorrow remains before us in this present age as a global barrier. 
Father, to overcome this barrier, we cannot do it alone as individuals. It cannot be done even with a few comrades who have a will. That is why You have gathered individuals to form families, gathered families to form tribes, gathered tribes to form nations, and gathered nations to establish a country. 
Even in forming a nation, Your desire has been for it to march toward a unified world. 
However, we must think that without individuals, families, tribes, and nations who can settle sin and take responsibility for Your work, it cannot be done. 
Even though the history of external sorrow has been created by people, how many of Your sons and daughters are there who are struggling to take responsibility for all of that on this earth for the world? 
Look upon Your children gathered here. Today, the children of unification are calling upon You, and they are struggling to establish the kingdom of heaven. But do we truly have the internal and external connections to call You "Father"? We must clearly recognize that we are not in a position to call upon You from a place where our hearts are united before Your will. 
When we call upon You with our flawed internal standards, flawed external standards, and flawed actions toward Your will, we must think about whether we have reached a position where You can joyfully welcome us, saying, "This is my son. This is my daughter." 
Rather, we realize that the voices we call out to You may be displeasing to Your ears, and that we often stand in a pitiful position where we can only be rejected before You. 
Even though we saw the sorrowful path of our Father, we did not know how to grieve, and even though we knew of Your earnest circumstances, we did not know how to struggle. 
Now, we must feel that the direction in which heaven and earth are moving is in such stark opposition, and that calling upon You from a place where our internal circumstances are in conflict cannot bring joy to Your heart. We may think that the place where we pray for blessings and receive blessings for You is a joyful place, but we have come to understand that it is not a place where You can rejoice. However, Father, how many of Your sons and daughters sincerely understand Your situation, who do not show signs of joy in joyful places and do not shy away from places where You are not joyful? 
Let this time be a moment where we reflect through our individual hearts and prepare ourselves anew before You. May we realize whether we have become individuals whom You can remember as having conditions and attitudes of compassion. 
Father! You are in pain, yet You answer our requests, waiting for a time when You can bless us. We must understand that. As we connect these days, we think about how deeply Your heart has been wounded over the 6,000 years of sorrowful history. 
Who can peel away this twisted and bound emotional sorrow? It must be true filial sons and true filial daughters. However, we know that it cannot be done with just filial sons centered on families, nor with just filial sons centered on tribes, nor with just filial sons representing nations. 
Unless we become true filial sons who can stand before Satan and boast on behalf of the world and heaven and earth, we cannot reveal the feelings that are hidden and embedded in Your heart. 
We sincerely hope and desire that You will forgive us for not having thought about the immense internal suffering You bear. 
Today is the Day of All Things, a day we commemorate. (The recording was briefly interrupted, and some parts could not be included.)
<Word> We can understand that when Adam and Eve fell, God experienced a psychological shock that humans could not feel. Of course, Adam and Eve must have felt an internal sorrowful shock when they were expelled from the garden of freedom. That shock must have been a combination of sorrowful emotions and shame before God. However, it was not the same for God. Rather, God was filled with a heart of indignation and sorrow over the fact that His purpose was not fulfilled. 
From that day and hour until now, history has been a continuous sorrow. Throughout this historical process, our ancestors have been called upon to fulfill their missions and responsibilities in each era. Thus, while those ancestors tried to fulfill their historical responsibilities, they ultimately left behind the responsibilities of their time unfulfilled for future generations. 
In this state, God has led history, and our ancestors have followed that history until now. 
The Fall of Humanity and God's Salvation Providence
However, there will come a time when those who bear historical missions will fulfill their responsibilities and achieve victory, thus establishing a new world. 
Looking back at the past, even though Jacob was called by God, he was not in a position to start freely. Jacob had a great mountain to overcome, which was to defeat his enemies. And to overcome that mountain, the family of Jacob, the tribe of Jacob, the nation of Israel, and the state of Israel had to overcome it together. 
If they had successfully crossed that mountain and reached the plains, the nation of Israel would have remained an eternal nation. However, they could not fulfill their responsibilities and retreated. Thus, even though they stood within the realm of blessings, they were pulled this way and that by many other nations, failing to fulfill their responsibilities before God. 
This is evident in the history of Israel. Therefore, they have never had a foundation of complete victory at any time. 
The name Israel appeared on this earth, but they could not find the name Israel that had won both inside and outside centered on the nation of Israel. They could not find a nation that could uphold the name Israel, nor could they establish the sovereignty to build the nation of Israel. 
That is why God's salvation providence has not yet had a day of victory. Thus, throughout the historical process, there have been times of rising and times of falling, times of striking Satan and times of being struck by Satan, expanding the form of history along with its flow. 
Therefore, the individual form has expanded into the family form, the family form has expanded into the tribal form, and the tribal form has been carried forward to the present global age. 
Then, has Christianity, which represents Israel, or the democratic world stood in the Abel position? 
…… There remains an external mountain that Christianity, representing Israel, must overcome, which is communism. Thus, today, the democratic world must successfully cross this mountain to reach the world of freedom and peace. Until that happens, we must clearly understand that God's providence cannot establish a global foundation. 
When individuals fail to carry out God's providence, He raises candidates to attach family providence, and when family providence fails, He raises candidates again to attach tribal providence. In this way, He has carried out national providence and global providence. 
So when will complete victory be determined both inside and outside? The purpose of Jesus coming to this earth 2,000 years ago was to establish the standard of internal victory in the Abel position and to fulfill His responsibilities before history by creating a solid external foundation. This was the mission of Jesus. He had to lead the surrounding Gentiles to God centered on the Jewish community and the nation of Israel in order to achieve victory. 
However, because Jesus could not overcome such a mountain and returned, while externally the world expanded, internally He could not establish a foundation for victory that could resolve individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, leaving it as a hope, and history has flowed down to this day.

The Holy Spirit like water
What kind of Holy Spirit is there? There is the Holy Spirit like fire, the Holy Spirit like a dove, the Holy Spirit like wind, the Holy Spirit like water, and the Holy Spirit like oil. But what is important in the human body? It is not the body that is important, but the heart. Then, what is necessary for a person to live? First, water is needed. Next, oil is needed. Finally, it refers to the dove, that is, the Holy Spirit. This is gentle and humble, does not get angry, and fits in with everything.

Today, Christian believers are seeking the Holy Spirit like water, the Holy Spirit like wind, and the Holy Spirit like clouds. This indicates that these are the most important things in this world. They are essential for sustaining life. Can a person live without breathing? Can they live without water? Can they live without oil? Oil is necessary for all joints to function. It is absolutely necessary. Therefore, how should we think about the properties of the Holy Spirit? When cooking or cleaning, the most important thing in living is water. Why do we use water? Because water always maintains a level. This water will always be at a 90-degree angle in front of the vertical center. It maintains the foundation that can be 90 degrees eternally.

Then, what does this vertical symbolize? It symbolizes heaven. Therefore, this water symbolizes the earth. This water will surely be received whenever God comes. Moreover, it does not move from the place where it is to be received. Thus, water symbolizes horizontal. Therefore, horizontal refers to an absolutely stable position that forms an eternal three-dimensional structure in relation to vertical.

Then, what is the Holy Spirit like water among the properties of the Holy Spirit on this earth? It means that it makes all people equally wide. Of course, water has various properties. The Holy Spirit like oil 
Next is oil. Is oil good or bad? "It's good." Then, is petroleum better or gasoline? For cars, is petroleum better or gasoline? They would say gasoline is better. Also, what does oil do? It acts as a lubricant. Similarly, when the Holy Spirit comes to this non-turning world and lubricates it, it starts to turn. Therefore, there is nothing that cannot be unified through the Holy Spirit. There is also nothing that cannot harmonize. No matter what situation arises, it happily flows along. Oil is like that. For someone with painful legs, oil must be applied. When a person becomes healthy, they gain strength. For that strength to arise, there must be oil in the body. Oil is an absolutely necessary element in our bodies. 

So what properties does oil have? Oil has a floating property. Isn't that right? Have you ever seen oil sink? For oil to float, it must be light. Is a person who is stubborn and heavy like a gentleman a heavy person or a light person? "A heavy person." A proud person cannot float. However, everyone should become a person who can float. Everyone should be mindful of this.

What is the nature of oil? It is neither stiff nor rough, but soft. 

In America, there is the Hoover Dam in the triangular area between California, Arizona, and Nevada. This world-class construction project cost 185 million dollars. For thousands of years, water flowing from several states has fallen into that one place. However, when that water falls on the rock, it has eroded it tremendously. The drop of this dam is 172 meters. There is a generator at this dam, and its output exceeds hundreds of thousands of kilowatts. That large generator spins at a considerable speed. The shaft of the generator contains bearings, and oil must be present for it to turn. Thus, ultimately, oil is indispensable for spinning that large generator. More urgent than spinning is the task of changing the oil. If the shaft and bearings come into contact, high heat will be generated. Therefore, although oil may seem insignificant, it ultimately drives the generator. 

Thus, oil-like elements are absolutely necessary in our Christianity. The properties of the Holy Spirit also have aspects like oil. 

The Holy Spirit like fire 
There are other aspects, but next is the Holy Spirit like fire. Even with something useless, if you apply a little force and rub it three times, fire can be created. Even when I was in prison, I could create fire with nothing. Even now, if I go to the mountains and gather a few things and rub them against a stone, fire can easily arise. This is because the Holy Spirit is present there. However, just shouting "Fire, catch!" does not create fire. Miracles do not happen that way. Therefore, for fire to ignite, you must quickly and diligently exchange energy. 

For you, heat is currently circulating through your blood vessels at a rapid speed. Heat does not arise if it remains still. It must be exchanged. 

What kind of person is happy? A person who has something to give, even if they have nothing to receive. However, a person who has something to receive but nothing to give is an unhappy person. A person recognized by God and advocating goodness does not receive help. Evil people, like beasts, try to receive but are unhappy.

Therefore, when all people give and take centered on life, heat arises. When heat arises, resurrection occurs. Thus, a new resurrection occurs through fire. When wood burns, it turns to ash and disappears, but a new resurrection occurs through fire. Isn't that so? That is why it is called the Holy Spirit like fire. 

The Holy Spirit like wind 
Next is the Holy Spirit like wind. Wind is created due to changes in air pressure. When it moves, it does not stop just because you tell it not to go. Typhoons occur due to the highest high pressure and the lowest low pressure. They cross oceans and even exceed the radius of the earth. They move with great vigor, even pushing aside enemies. I like typhoons. 

A few years ago, while I was fishing on a boat, I encountered a strong wind. The boat was damaged, tossed around by waves, and rain hit my face, making it sting, but I felt very good. **The Boundary of Heart**  
<Summary of the Words> The world is currently facing a very difficult period. At the peak of the confrontation between democracy and communism, the question is how our Unification Church will become the center and advance. 

To achieve the ideals of humanity, what is the first issue in pioneering the global course of the Unification Church? Of course, there will be economic issues and national issues. However, the greater issue is the issue of ideology. 

Even with many problems, to solve those problems, true human beings are needed. Then, what is necessary to be a true human being? It is precisely heart (emotion). 

Even if there is a true person here, they cannot stand in a position to say, "I am truly a globally happy person." The significant issue that allows one to stand in such a position is heart. 

To become a true human being, love becomes the issue. However, even if there is a person who has resolved the issue of love, that person cannot solve global problems. 

Therefore, to resolve this issue, it must ultimately lead to the issue of God's heart. 

Love is necessary for humans. However, love is not something that can be easily grasped or discarded; it is not that simple. 

When a person in love stands in a position opposite to oneself, how will the issue of love be resolved? If each insists only on their own position, it cannot be resolved. The issue of love has a relative relationship, so it must be discussed together to resolve it because that love is not an individual possession. 

The love of a parent for a child cannot be interfered with by anyone. There is a unique and absolute love as a parent. However, that does not mean it can be done freely. Love operates under certain laws with absolute authority, and even the parents themselves feel this. Therefore, the love of a parent for a child is not the parent's own love. 

So, who is the true owner of that love? 

It is neither the love of those who are in love nor the love of the parents who love their children, so we can say that love must not start from human beings themselves. When we delve into this issue, we inevitably conclude that the starting point of that love is indeed God.
If that love belongs to Adam or the archangel, it cannot be considered a sin simply because it was done as one pleases. It is a sin because it belongs to an absolute realm that cannot be acted upon freely. If we accept God's love from an honest perspective, our human society would not be in a position starving for love. However, what does the world resulting from the fall seek? It may be seeking happiness on a national level or prosperity centered around economic, political, and social issues. But the greater issue is that all countries and peoples of the world do not realize that the problem of love, which can lead society on a holy path, is far more important.

Therefore, God has raised one person to give humanity the love that can communicate His heart, establishing a relationship between heaven and earth, and creating a point of peace. This is the history of restoration providence. This is the central issue of God's providence.

No matter how much wealth one possesses, standing at the pinnacle of that wealth cannot bring satisfaction. One cannot feel true happiness unless they have resolved the issue of love. Thus, the fundamental issue that can achieve humanity's ideals is the issue of love.

The trend of communism in Japan and our stance.  
<Summary of the words> When the teacher went to Japan last time, he felt that the hearts of the Japanese members towards the homeland of faith must be unified.  
Until now, we have moved around centered on missionaries who are engaged in missionary activities abroad, so it seems we could not proceed in one direction consistently. I thought that if we left this as it is, as time goes on, it would have a negative impact on all members, and I was also concerned. This time, I brought the headquarters' executives to Japan to send them to each region to establish emotional ties with the Japanese members. This was the plan I had when I took the executives with me.  
From now on, Korea must also unite as a nation.  
So, upon arriving in Japan, we held a training session for two weeks, and afterward, we toured the regions for 13 days. After that, I visited most of Japan's important factories.  
The reason is that while the religious issue and faith movement are important for us, we must also keep in mind the grand goal of national development in Korea and plan accordingly.  
Therefore, I visited more than ten factories to see the current situation of the Japanese industry. What I felt there was that Korea must now unite as a nation.  
When looking at industrial issues, it feels late for Korea to surpass Japan. They have already reached a world level in various fields, and if they produce goods through the factories scattered throughout Japan, those goods can be supplied throughout Asia. I could imagine that if Japan develops for another ten years, Europeans will also suffer considerable hardships because of Japan.  
Thinking of this, I considered the development issues of Korea, and I felt that we must set grand plans and engage in new fields. Even aside from the Unification Church as an organization, if the 30 million people of our nation unite and confront Japan, which is dominating Asia, we must tighten our belts and work tirelessly for the next 20 to 30 years to surpass them.  
Also, I was worried about how we could elevate our nation to a position comparable to Japan.  
While we have been active centered around the Unification Church in Korea, the anti-communist lectures we have conducted have now developed to the point of growing to a national level.  
From this perspective, the position we are in now is one where we are responsible for the anti-communist system in Asia and are leading the fight, so I cannot help but feel how lonely this position is. In other words, we have no comrades.  
The issue of involving Japan in the anti-communist front.  
Looking at the current situation in Korea, the Soviet Union and China surround us, while North Korea is waiting for an opportunity to invade the South.  
On the other hand, Japan is currently divided into three factions politically.  
The leftist faction, the rightist faction, and a middle political force that seems to represent the democratic camp and also the independent line of Japan can clearly be seen as divided into these three factions.  
When you go to Tokyo, you can see the sign of the Japanese Communist Party boldly displayed in red letters in the city. They confidently promote communism even during the day at Tokyo Station and Shibuya Station.  
In the Japanese National Assembly, communist members are working together with the Socialist Party to fight against the Liberal Democratic Party. They oppose everything proposed by the Liberal Democratic Party, and they are conducting joint operations in the National Assembly. In fact, there are no conditions to oppose, but they do so to solidify their underground base by rallying Japanese communists and all workers and farmers as a tool for their use. I feel that communists are obsessed with such things.  
Currently, the number of formal communist party members in Japan is estimated to be between 130,000 and 170,000. However, the number of people who can engage in collective action centered around them reaches as high as 2.8 million to 3.5 million.  
This force is dispersed throughout Japan and is continuously active, and among them, the most cunning and malicious group belongs to the Chosun Soren (Korean Residents Union in Japan). They are active as the action troops of the Communist Party. This is the current situation in Japan.  
Currently, the Korean Embassy in Japan has a national mission both administratively and politically, so it cannot establish direct relations with the Korean Residents Union and is working from an intermediary position.  
By taking a position equal to that of the Japanese government politically, if they engage in the activities of the Residents Union, it would hinder their own activities, so they are standing in an intermediary position.  
The Residents Union itself is budgeting about 30 million won for the upcoming August 15 event. To secure this funding, the leaders of the Residents Union must go to the wealthy Korean residents behind them every time to solicit contributions.  
However, how are the Communist Party and North Korea connected? North Korea has invested over 5 billion won in the Japanese Communist Party and is launching an offensive. Therefore, whenever Korean students go to Japan to study, they are eager to provide scholarships unconditionally to absorb them into the Communist Party.  
Because of this reality, we cannot establish an anti-communist system focused solely on Korea to confront the communist front scattered throughout Asia. The question of how to involve Japan in this anti-communist front has been a problem the teacher has been considering until now.  
The first anti-communist lecture in Japan, which was achieved with great difficulty.  
So, the teacher thought that he must find a way, and as soon as he arrived in Japan, he visited the embassy and the Residents Union, presenting the achievements of the anti-communist lectures conducted in the homeland, and proposed to conduct anti-communist lectures centered around the Korean residents in Japan.
It was a strong demand that it had to be done. In response, the embassy took a high-handed stance as the representative of the country, while the Mindan side, standing in the position of representing 600,000 overseas Koreans, also adopted a high-handed attitude, claiming that their leaders were not envious of any Korean minister. 

However, heaven sent Choi Chang-rim, the district head, to that place. Although District Head Choi could not speak Japanese, he appointed a person named Jo to serve as an interpreter. This Jo was originally one of the key figures who led the organization of the Mindan when it was established, taking advantage of the opportunity for the Koreans in Japan to unite when Park Cheol, a contributor to its founding, came out. After that, he felt that in order to carry out significant activities in Japan, an economic foundation was necessary. So he left the work of the Mindan and devoted himself to business, and this time he served as the interpreter for District Head Choi. 

First, District Head Choi was to give a lecture at a gathering of about 450 representatives from women's associations across 47 prefectures in Japan. He repeatedly emphasized to the deputy head that it was essential to conduct anti-communist lectures for the overseas Koreans in the future. 

On the day of the national women's association conference, I went to see the deputy head, and at that moment, the deputy head, the director of the cultural department, and the director of the organizational department were about to get into a car to head to the conference venue. When I asked, "Where are you going?" they replied, "We are on our way to the national women's conference." I said, "What should we do? We came to meet you, and we can't just turn back," and they suggested that we go together, so we headed straight to the conference venue. 

By the time we arrived at the venue, which was just about to start, I had already made some arrangements with a few people there, so it was concluded that it would be good to hear District Head Choi's lecture once. 

Upon arriving there, District Head Choi greeted the person in charge of the meeting and engaged in serious persuasion with him for about 30 minutes. He started by explaining the origin of the organization called Seonggong Gyeongmyeongdan that came from the homeland. He explained that it was a group that might be unknown if one were to inquire with the government, but it had influenced all of South Korea and had impacted every household. He insisted that since the women were not ideologically prepared, they needed to be awakened. 

Thus, he obtained 20 minutes to give a lecture at the national women's representatives' conference. At that time, the embassy and the Mindan first introduced themselves, and after a few people from the women's association came out to greet, District Head Choi went out to give his lecture. During the 20-minute lecture, he received applause a remarkable twelve times. 

As a result, the audience was captivated by the lecture, and they said they had never seen such a small gentleman speak so well. The person in charge of the meeting and the Mindan leaders also expressed that they were profoundly impressed. This became a good opportunity for us to work with peace of mind, and we negotiated daily for the holding of anti-communist lectures. 

In conducting anti-communist lectures, it may be necessary to expose the realities of North Korea by former spies or people who were repatriated, but that would only have a temporary effect. Even if those people talk about how Kim Il-sung is and what the situation in North Korea is like, it would just be vague statements that cannot be believed from the perspective of Japan. Such statements would rather lead people to think that the South Korean government has manipulated them and applied pressure, forcing them to speak that way. 

They already knew that such outdated anti-communist measures were ineffective. Therefore, they argued that we could not rely on such an approach. They actively explained and emphasized that we should lecture by fundamentally dissecting communism, presenting the content that communism is bad and that historically or temporally, it must inevitably fail. 

Impressing Overseas Korean Students
After that, the Mindan side contacted us to say that a summer gathering of overseas Korean students in Nagoya would be held for four days in a coastal area, and they would give us a chance to go and try it out as a pilot case. So, with the introduction of the Mindan headquarters, we went there. 

There was one president and three vice presidents among the executives, and these three vice presidents opposed our lecture. So, I tearfully appealed, saying that I had come all the way from Korea with great expectations for the young people in Japan, but I never expected this! The president was deeply moved and sympathized with us. All decision-making authority there rested with the president and vice presidents, and then eight executives would hold a meeting to make resolutions. However, since all three vice presidents opposed it, the president could not assert his position. 

With no other choice, the president hurriedly ran upstairs to gather the eight heads and said, "A famous teacher from the homeland has come, and I think it would be good for the students to hear a lecture, even if just for a few minutes, but the vice presidents are opposed, and I'm in a difficult position. What do you all think?" They responded that it would be good to listen. Thus, the heads gathered all the students together. 

As a result, the vice presidents, whose position had become awkward, fled the scene. Later, it turned out that these people were all pro-North Korean leftists. 

Most of them were students who had entered Japan through smuggling and were receiving economic support from North Korea while expanding their activities by recruiting overseas Korean students and taking on vice president positions, thus spreading such underground organizations. This fact was belatedly uncovered due to this incident. This incident triggered a massive investigation into overseas Korean students throughout Japan. 

In any case, delivering a passionate speech for about 40 minutes to the students gathered at this summer gathering yielded great results. The Mindan vice president, the head of the cultural department, and the head of the organization, who had accompanied me, were all impressed. According to them, they had invited many lecturers to Japan to give lectures to overseas Koreans, but all had ended without any significant effect. However, this time, District Head Choi's lecture was welcomed by both the women's association and the younger people, which was quite unusual. 

To elaborate on the situation at that time, the moderator initially came out and tried to speak for about five minutes. At that point, the students began to stomp their feet on the floor and shout for him to stop. With over 200 students present, they were not there to listen to such trivial talk, and they shouted to clear the stage, putting their feet up on the chairs and creating a chaotic atmosphere. 

In such a situation, the small-statured District Head Choi took the stage. Given that he seemed like he could fly away, one can imagine the feelings of those who had accompanied him. The district head of the Unification Church in Nagoya, who was Japanese, witnessed that scene and thought that since the moderator was being chased away, District Head Choi would surely be chased away within a minute. He was so anxious that he could not help but pray. 

However, as soon as District Head Choi took the stage, he began to bombard them with words like a bomb from the very beginning. He talked about the current state of universities in Korea, the situation in the country, and how Unification Church members were struggling and sweating for the nation, while the young students were also worrying and shedding tears for their country, and he reproached them with tears, questioning how the Korean students in Japan, who were expected to have the most hope, could be in such a state. 

After about five minutes of this, their feet, which had been propped up on the chairs, had come down, and the venue had quieted down as if water had been poured on it, and the place was all organized. 

After the lecture, which felt like a beating for about 40 minutes, all the student executives rushed to meet the lecturer, eager to receive his business card. They introduced themselves, saying, "I am the president of such and such university," or "I attend such and such university," thus revealing their identities. This opened up a clear path for us there as well. 

Invitation to the August 15 Commemoration Event
The Mindan side mentioned that they were inviting lecturers for the August 15 commemoration event, and while they needed other people, they particularly needed someone to give an anti-communist lecture. 

However, in Japan, even during the day, the communists are rampant, so if one criticizes the communists, one does not know what might happen. After two days of back-and-forth, they decided to cancel the other eight people and put forward just District Head Choi and one other person. They also decided that a commemorative lecture would be held at 10 o'clock during the event.

They decided to sharply criticize the inner workings of communism and instill a deep awareness of communism, believing that afterward, the Japanese would support the anti-communist lectures we were conducting. 

Then, you must clearly understand why this must be done. Looking at the political situation in Japan, the Social Democratic Party has 111 seats in the National Assembly. What will happen to Japan in 1970? Japan, which has been under the guidance of the United States, will likely adopt a position of independence once it breaks free from the protective treaty. This will undoubtedly make communism a significant issue in Japan. The Liberal Democratic Party, which has maintained a pro-American relationship based on democracy, will eventually manifest in three forms: a democratic line, a communist line, and a nationalistic domestic line. 

In this situation, Japan will not be able to accept just anything. They will have to adopt one of the left or right positions or their own national line. In other words, they will inevitably face a situation where they must make a decision. 

Given this reality in Japan, how will the communist countries, namely the Soviet Union and China, respond? 

Until now, Japan has been paired with the United States, so they have not been able to engage in effective agitation or operations, nor have they taken any active actions. However, what they desire is that by 1970, Japan, which is still under the protection of the security treaty, will be freed from American protection, and until then, they will do everything possible to push Japan into an anti-American stance. 

The communists are now watching for that opportunity. 

What policies will the Soviet Union and China adopt to seize such an opportunity? They will import goods produced in Japan, even if they do not need them, to closely establish friendly relations with Japan. The reason is to widen the gap between Japan and the United States as much as possible.

If China were to import all of Japan's production resources and solidify its military base centered on key industries, it would not leave Japan alone. So, what will China do to achieve that goal? Most of the trade goods that Japan exports to Southeast Asia, the Middle East, or Europe go through the Taiwan Strait. Therefore, around 1970, China might invade Taiwan to block this route. 

If they were to occupy Taiwan within three to seven days, military aid through congressional resolution in the United States would already be too late. If China occupies Taiwan, the Taiwan Strait will be completely sealed off, and as a result, over 60% of Japan's trade will be interrupted, leading to an economic chaos that will suddenly spread within Japan. 

Isn't this their scheme to create a foundation for a communist revolution in Japan? If Japan falls into such a state, Korea will inevitably become a rat in a trap.

Love and reciprocal action  
Today, regardless of communism or democracy, scientists say that this universe, this nature, is made of matter. Then, what is matter made of? Matter is made of force. However, force cannot arise by itself. Force also does not emerge unless there is an action of giving and receiving, as relative standards cannot be established without it. The force that acts and arises in your body comes from the giving and receiving among your limbs. The force emerges in proportion to that giving and receiving.  
Before there is force, there must be an action of giving and receiving. So, what must happen for there to be an action of giving and receiving? One cannot absolutely perform an action of giving and receiving alone. This is undeniable. Therefore, to perform an action of giving and receiving, a counterpart is absolutely necessary. This is an absolute requirement for all forms of existence. Without a counterpart, there can be no giving and receiving.  
For this reason, for a person to exist, they must first go through a process of giving and receiving starting from their own body. Men and women must have relative conditions to give and receive from each other to exist. If men say they do not need women, and women say they do not need men, the world will perish within a century. For people to exist, that is, to give and receive, they need a counterpart, which is why men and women have loved each other and formed families until now. Thus, love is the force that generates the action of giving and receiving. It is the force of the action of giving and receiving between men and women.  
Therefore, for the force of love to arise, there must be an action of giving and receiving, and for there to be an action of giving and receiving, men and women are absolutely necessary. That is, the requirement for a counterpart is needed.  
How did the universe initially start? What was the starting point of its development until now? It did not originate from the struggles arising from contradictions as communists claim, but began from the establishment of relative relationships. That is, the universe began to emerge from the pursuit of relative relationships.  
For instance, if someone is trying to go to Myeongdong without a relative purpose, then that step becomes meaningless. The actions of going and coming must occur centered around relative conditions. Without a counterpart, no action can occur. And if no action occurs, force cannot emerge. Therefore, the essence of the universe must also have relative conditions.  
Then, will the relative conditions act in a negative (-), that is, in a loss-making manner, or will they act in a positive (+), that is, in a profit-making manner? If someone is going somewhere to incur a loss, that person is not a normal person. A normal person is one who goes when there is a positive (+) condition that benefits them. Therefore, there is absolutely no one who moves to engage in an action of giving and receiving with the intention of incurring a loss.  
If we examine the actions of the elements that make up matter, we can see that for two elements to combine, there must be better conditions than before they combine. In other words, they will not act unless they discover a value that can help them.  
322   Universal support for a unified world  
From this perspective, the dialectic, which claims that contradictions act against each other, is fundamentally incorrect. The young men and women passing through Myeongdong may seem to be going back and forth for no reason, but they are doing so because there are conditions that provide a positive (+) benefit for them. They come and go to make even a mere 100 won profit each day; no one moves to incur a loss.

God's creation of heaven and earth also unfolded to discover conditions that could yield positive (+) outcomes. This is a principle.

God's love becomes the source of unity. When this love is brought forth, it generates the power to embrace all nations, and even if it holds all nations forever, it desires to embrace them even more.

Love, just like a parent loves a child, increases joy the more it is expressed. Love is unity. If there is love that is united with God's love, that love cannot be separated by anyone. How wonderful is that love?

The loss of such love is the fall. Therefore, through the truth taught by the Unification Church, we must first understand God's love and then make God's love our own. Furthermore, we must recognize God, who rejoices at seeing us through that love. If we do not know this, we have love, but it is a love that is not needed by us.

If we do not know whether we are liked or disliked, that love will break apart. Especially for women, a husband's love is the most important. Even if they hear "I love you" countless times, they want to hear it again. Why? Because the ancestor of humanity sowed the seeds of love at an inappropriate time.

The Unification Church introduces God's love and shows the way to possess that love so that one can come to a place where they can rejoice in front of that love. If the Unification Church did not have such content but still put up the sign of the Unification Church, then the person known as the leader of the Unification Church would be a fraud. Unification is not about being dragged along; it is about pulling and unifying through oneself. When there is a lovable person, everyone gathers from all around. If there is a beauty that captivates the world, all men will be interested and gather around. That is why once you enter the Unification Church, you will be drawn to it.

Humans lost God's love due to the fall. The relationships formed without God's love are the fall, and the love connections we form in the world today are loves that the original nature of humanity cannot long for. That love is all love that will melt away on earth.

Therefore, when one goes to the spirit world, even couples who had a good relationship on earth become strangers. They will surely be separated. However, couples who started without falling and were united by God's love can never be separated.

People Who Can Enter Heaven
Heaven is the place where couples who are completely united centered on God's love enter, and it is where the children born from those united couples, that is, families, tribes, and nations united around God, all enter. Therefore, Jesus, who did not have a family on earth, has not been able to enter heaven and remains in paradise until now. Only couples united by God's love can enter heaven. Heaven is a world of relative ideals. Therefore, families must all enter, and their tribes and nations must all enter. That is how heaven is established.

Until now, no one has been able to enter heaven. Everyone is waiting in the waiting room for heaven. The door of God's love has not yet opened, so the door to heaven cannot be opened. That is why Jesus came to open this door to heaven, but He could not meet the relative reality on earth. In other words, the relative subject that could be a plus (+) to Jesus' love has not appeared. That is why Jesus has been walking the path of labor for 2,000 years, longing for the day when the door to heaven will be opened. On the day of His second coming, He will choose one bride from among all people to open the door of God's love and enter.

However, Christians who do not know this are the real heretics. There will come a time when they will be caught. If that time does not come, the teacher will make it happen. They may feel uncomfortable hearing this, but they will inevitably be caught. Among those who have come here for the first time, there may be some who were Christians and have had experiences opposing the Unification Church. The lady over there also opposed the Unification Church but repented and went out to evangelize. The Unification Church is forgiving because it has a lot of compassion and a great outreach.

The weather is hot, and lunchtime has passed, so you must be hungry. However, the teacher has not eaten breakfast. It is best to fast when feeling unwell. Try keeping your mouth shut for a day or two. You do not need medicine.

What kind of power should Unification Church members have? They must pump their hearts strongly to cultivate the power to drag the body along. The problem is uniting those who have already been born with that power.

Unity can only be achieved centered on God's love. Therefore, the truth of the Unification Church makes God's love known to all people and allows them to possess that love. It also teaches them to understand what position they are in within God's love. Regardless of whether they are black, white, or yellow, all people have the same heart. That is why the conclusion arises that all nations must be unified.

The Unification Church must build the heart world that all people desire.
What if this place were only about one-fifth of its current size? Then everyone would have to stand for five or six hours to worship. At that time, a true Unification Church member would worship even while standing. If that happens, people will flock to this place in huge numbers.

However, the strange thing is that when people come to the Unification Church, their own homes feel like their neighbors' homes, and this sweaty church feels like their own home. So, would you prefer to live in your neighbor's house or your own? Everyone wants to live in the Unification Church, which feels like a neighbor's house, so the teacher receives a lot of criticism. However, if the teacher prays for Unification Church members, a strong power is activated. What has been taught is to break down everything that has been lived up to now. Thus, a world of emotional dimensions that was previously unimaginable has begun to unfold.

People think that when they hear about the leader of the Unification Church, he is sitting in a high position and giving orders. However, those who have come to the Unification Church say the atmosphere is so free that sometimes it feels like the top is the bottom and the bottom is the top, which can be confusing. A newcomer may not know who the teacher is and usually thinks the association president is the teacher. Today, since the teacher has come out like this, they may recognize him, but if they were sitting in the back, new arrivals would not have known that I am the teacher of the Unification Church. Our Unification Church atmosphere is indeed very free. It is truly a place of liberation. Therefore, there is liberation at home and liberation in the nation. Intelligent people born in the Republic of Korea, a small nation, have lamented being born into this ethnicity. However, that lament will all disappear.

To the teacher, even a great leader who has unified the world seems like a pebble rolling at his feet. Did God send the teacher to this earth just to put a crown on his head and make him dance? When viewed in light of God's will, it is undoubtedly a fact that the teacher has been doing sincere work in the world he has fought, pioneered, and built. No matter how much anyone lies, the historical evidence is as massive as a mountain, making it undeniable.

Do not be afraid of being criticized for believing in the Unification Church. Criticism comes in and goes out, so there is no need to worry. Criticism is like a tree swaying in the wind. It feels worse to be praised than to be criticized. It is fitting for a man’s temperament to boast after doing something that others say cannot be done; simply obeying from the beginning does not suit a man’s temperament and is not fun. From this perspective, the path of the Unification Church fits the temperament of the teacher perfectly.

Communists aim for a material paradise as their highest goal. However, those who believe in love, the most precious thing in the world, that is, those who are in God's love, know that a material paradise is not the highest goal. Therefore, the theories of communism will be shattered because of the emergence of the Unification Church.

For the sake of God's love, the husband is not a problem, nor is the family a problem. There will be times when the whole world weeps for the ideal of seeking God's kingdom and His righteousness; at that time, Unification Church members will stand as those who can commemorate the loyalty and integrity of filial piety for eternity. Therefore, you must understand that the value of Unification Church members cannot be compared to worldly success, hope, and happiness.

Unification must begin from my body and heart. The Unification Church teaches this. Thus, when you come out of the Unification Church, even those who were distant like strangers become closer than brothers. Furthermore, it possesses a higher love that can unite not only different siblings but also different nations and different ethnicities more strongly than physical parents.

That is why this place cannot help but be called the world of universal support and unification. By entering the Unification Church, you can acquire the elements of this hope.

The Mission of Heavenly Warriors
The Unification Church teaches not only the ideal love of God but also the sorrowful heart of God that has appeared throughout the historical process. Those who do not know history cannot understand reality, and those who do not understand reality cannot know the future. The same goes for knowing God. Without knowing the God of the past, one cannot know the God of today.

The image of a Unification warrior must be one that seeks the joys and sorrows hidden within God's love and expresses them in reality, running toward humanity with God's love. This is the absolute requirement for unity that must be clearly understood.

That is why, on this path, there will be times when the world will persecute us, and we must overcome this. Until now, those who have attended the Unification Church have been the targets of criticism and ridicule. However, if we go just a little further, we will proclaim all the falsehoods through the mass media. If the teacher cannot buy the Seoul Central Broadcasting Station, he will establish a larger broadcasting station. That time will surely come. At that time, just give the teacher the microphone for three days.

You must become heavenly warriors to create such an enormous world and become heavenly messengers, aiming only for victory. You must go to the country where victory dwells and meet the Father in the world where victory dwells.

Therefore, Unification warriors must understand that no matter how long the path of struggle is or how arduous the march may be, they must not lose heart on that path. The teacher is at the forefront, working to fulfill the wishes of the world of universal support and unification. This conviction of the teacher is to lead you, even if it means scolding and hitting you, to that world. If you do not want to go, you will be made to go.
are trying to pull the cart. Even so, do you have the confidence to follow? This path is one that I do not know well at the moment, but if you think about it, it is actually a path filled with worries. There is no day to sleep comfortably, and there is no time to sit down and eat peacefully. This is because we must sacrifice for the whole. We must not leave any strength behind. If there is even a little energy left to pour out, we must continue to move forward. 

Is there anyone among you who finds listening to the teacher's words boring? There may be those who feel bored, but if there are even ten people who do not feel that way, the teacher must speak for those ten people. This path is not a simple ideological revolution. The Unification Church aims to transfer the emotional content received from fallen ancestors to a higher world of love, like a whirlwind. Therefore, there is no time to rest on the path we are taking. The role of the Unification Church teacher cannot be replaced by anyone else. Not even the most famous doctor in the world can do it. If it is not the teacher, then no one can do it. Because of this teacher, I can say that I will use you as workers. 

When the teacher returned from abroad and landed at Gimpo Airport, looking at Korea, my heart ached, and I cried inside. The teacher often cried while looking at Korea during school days. If the plan to establish this purpose before this nation and the world had been fulfilled back then, what would this country be like now? Thinking about that, it is inevitable that my heart aches again as I approach fifty. If the plans made during my school days had been realized, this country would not have become so desolate. Since this nation does not recognize the Unification Church, it must be done by the teacher's strength. 

If there had been no Unification Church in Korea, the future of Korea could not be guaranteed even for a single day. Moreover, if the Unification Church had not emerged from the East, Japan would not be able to solve the communist problem no matter how hard it tried. 

When I think like this, you who belong to the Unification Church have a mission to save this nation. Therefore, you must maintain the heart of your parents and uphold the mission of pioneers. I also hope you will pledge to run towards tomorrow's victory while organizing each day. 

With the words you have heard so far, you must establish a world of love and goodness where God can dwell before God. Therefore, I ask you to fulfill the responsibility of heavenly warriors who conquer the difficulties and evils of the world. 

<Prayer> Upon returning to the land of Korea and standing on my homeland, looking at the tearful family members, I know that the Father understands the sorrowful circumstances that fill my heart. 

If our hearts are like this, what must the Father's heart be like? I earnestly hope that the Father will have compassion on us, who are ashamed to appeal our sorrows before Him, and allow us to once again envision the Father of mercy and compassion. 

Father, I reflect on how the name of the Father, which many people have called, has been proven today through the Unification Church, and how the Father’s image has been revealed. I cannot help but worry that we may leave a shock of sorrow before the Father, who has hope for us amidst the twists and turns of eternal grief. 

Our decades-long journey has been a path of struggle, a path of writhing amidst the sorrowful twists of the cross, but we know that the Father has walked a path of suffering a million times more than ours. Remembering the sorrow of today, I discover my own shortcomings, and I hope that the Father will look upon these hearts with affection. 

At this time, many children are bowing before the Father. Whom do their hearts long for? For whom do they become bowed bodies? And whose life do they live for? It is undoubtedly for the Father, and it is certain that they are returning to the Father. This nation is a nation with complicated stories and circumstances, a nation that yearns for the Father and can harmonize with the Father’s love. Therefore, we have realized that becoming a dutiful child who can comfort the Father with relative achievements is the focal point of our issues. When that day comes, the Father will be with us, and what belongs to the Father will become ours. 

We have learned that before lamenting the world, we must lament ourselves. We must create ourselves that cannot help but rise and explode with the Father's heart and love. Let these children realize that it is time to have the strength to transcend the nation and cross the seas, circling this globe. 

Father! When I see Your children in a position where they cannot love You, I feel that there is a need for Your whip and the strong guidance and counsel of a sorrowful Father. However, seeing that there is no one who can act in Your stead, I earnestly hope that each of us can take on that role. 

Father, please remember the thirty million people of this nation. May the traces of blood and tears shed by Your children in every corner of the three thousand ri not be occupied by Satan as a foundation for curses. Please raise up future generations who can call upon You on that holy foundation, so that we can welcome a day of glory and establish a holy sanctuary to serve the Father and praise the victory of happiness. 

This is our wish, and today we must work for it, tomorrow we must work for it, and we must dedicate our entire lives to it. Therefore, we must die in that place of dedication if we must die. However, we know that the issue of life and death should not be a concern for ourselves, but rather, let our only concern be for the remaining purpose, I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father. 

If there are children among those gathered here today who are seeing the teacher for the first time, may they discover a new appearance that can yearn for a world with a childlike heart and return. May they think about how great and amazing the content of that value is and return as the children of the Father who have discovered the value of life in this place, I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father. 

Today is a holy day, so please bless it. In every corner of the Korean Peninsula, may those who hold onto the Father's heart with lonely tears and declare a warning to the pitiful world of Satan be protected. 

May the traces of their sweat, tears, and blood be eternally occupied by the Father, and may He dwell there. 

Please allow us to erect the sign of victory, and may there be descendants of a good nation who can inherit it forever, even if only that desire remains, I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father. 

Please remember the many children who have been left behind in Japan. Even if they are in a place where the wind blows and storms rage, may the Father be completely the master among them, and with Your hand and will, embrace them so that they may avoid places of injury. 

May the Father directly comfort the children who shed tears yearning for the teacher of the homeland and become their master. We must not prioritize national feelings, but rather unite for the world of hope centered around heavenly content. Because this is a way to serve the Father, may You personally dwell there and be the master of today, the master of this year, and the master of their lives. I hope and wish that You will personally govern and protect us. 

I earnestly hope that You will remember the many brothers scattered throughout the world. 

I earnestly hope that everything that will happen from today onward will fulfill the will that the Father is orchestrating and prepare a foundation that can present the victory of equality before all people. I earnestly wish for this, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

**Direction of the Interdenominational Movement**  
<Summary of the Words> The reason the teacher is currently in Pal-dang is to distribute to established churches, just as Jacob settled his 21-year period and shared his wealth with Esau. In other words, it is to complete Jacob's blessing. Therefore, this period is one in which our family must sacrifice everything to give to established church members. 

We have a mission to help the families of martyrs who are in difficult situations while being loyal to God in established churches. 

We should have great interest in the interdenominational movement and be able to support at least thirty million won by next spring. 

The issue is how the district leaders will have a heart that resembles the emotional heart of spring. Just as the land can welcome spring because it has become a foundation for it, the district leaders must establish such a heart and tradition. 

Since the teacher could not travel the world, he plans to stay here in Pal-dang until the end of September. 

Now, we must raise a new movement centered on the heart. 

Where I am going is also a problem for the teacher. 

Without the heart of a parent, one cannot find their children. The principle of the purpose must stand above one's own children. There must be a greater interest and concern for the church than for the family. 

September 4, 1967 (Monday), Pal-dang, Gyeonggi Province.  
* These words were spoken during a district leaders' meeting and are compiled from notes recorded by former President Yoo Ho-won. The title was added by the editor. 

Just as the teacher met with the members when leaving Pyongyang and walked a new path, the teacher must now welcome new members and start anew. 

**Father and I**  
<Summary of the Words> The father-son relationship between the Father, who should be the center of the universe, and I has been severed due to the Fall. 

Let us become loyal subjects and dutiful children who devote our hearts, intentions, and character. 

The Fall is not external. It is because we lost the internal emotional connection with the Father that humanity cannot stand before God. Therefore, I must comfort God on the foundation of restoring the lost internal heart and stand on that standard myself. This is God's ultimate providence. Thus, the restoration providence has emerged by clearing away everything that opposes this path. 

Because we have lost the Father's heart, we must walk the path of faith to restore it. However, this path of restoration is infinitely close in the emotional world, yet it is a distant path because we have strayed from the emotional world. You must understand that many historical figures have shed tears of blood and made sacrifices to shorten this distance. Therefore, the day must come when we can gather and connect the entirety of the restoration providence that our ancestors sacrificed for. 

God has desired that humanity love Him with all their heart, intention, and character. However, if even one person remains who does not do so, He cannot fulfill His purpose. That is why He commanded us to love our neighbors as ourselves. 

Humanity must become individuals who can represent the spiritual world and heaven and earth in order to establish a new historical point. Therefore, we must realize that the spirits of our ancestors are watching us. We must reflect on where we stand based on this standard. 

God desires all people to be dutiful children and loyal subjects. Furthermore, God desires those who stand at the highest standard among them. God hopes for those who say there is no other way but the path of loyalty and duty. 

You must occupy a higher position than anyone else in the historical course. In other words, you must stand in a position that is ahead of anyone in the historical course, such as Abel's emotional standard and Noah's 120 years of sincerity. The standard of loyalty and duty to God transcends history. 

You must surely realize that you are the sons and daughters of God. It is not a matter of whether you can fight well; rather, it is whether you have become someone who can be loved. The representative figure of that is Jesus. He is the historical fruit. Jesus intended to do everything centered on the heart. Therefore, we must become the historical reality of the resurrection of Christ. It is as such that we must stand before God. 

The path that the teacher has re-pioneered is the path he has walked for over thirty years. It is a path that comforts God's heart. The group gathered for this purpose is the group of unification. 

Now, two-thirds of the last year of the seven-year course has passed. We have gone through many adversities during this time. Even to the point of abandoning our homes, we worked for God's will to emulate the example of Jesus. 

The position you are currently in is not the position that heaven and earth desire. You must become the dutiful children that your parents desire. You must serve heaven with all your heart, intention, and character. A dutiful child and loyal subject is one who dedicates their heart, intention, and character. That position is the standard recognized by God. There is no greater disloyalty than wanting to be treated as if you are in that position while you are not. 

You must surpass the emotional standard of Adam before the Fall. There is no greater disloyalty than wanting something beyond that while you cannot stand in the position that God desires. 

Those who cannot take responsibility for their parents' lives and property and bring peace and development to their families cannot be dutiful children. When the parents' property is in danger, one must be able to throw away everything for it. 

Since God's ideal of creation has been shattered, one cannot be a loyal subject or dutiful child in a place that violates life, property, peace, and ideals. When have I ever felt as anxious for God as I do for my own matters? When have I ever felt a sense of mission regarding my Father's life? When have I ever struggled and fought for the peace and unity of my Father's family? I have asked myself these questions, but they have not become loyalty and duty before God; they have become disloyalty and disrespect. 

One must think that what belongs to the individual is the church's, what belongs to the church is the nation's, and what belongs to the nation is the world, heaven, and God's. Nevertheless, there is a growing tendency for many to think only of their own possessions. 

There has not been a single loyal subject among those who have claimed their own possessions and themselves throughout the historical course. 

Let us run to the end, prepared for death. 

Unification members must stand in a position to sacrifice themselves to defeat Satan in the end. When God's property is in danger, one must become the one who sacrifices in place of it. At this critical juncture of the last seven-year course, the teacher cannot help but say these words to you. 

As this course passes, the teacher cannot suppress his sorrow. The teacher also reflects on himself and carries a heavy heart. He has thought about the scene of Jesus disappearing in tragedy millions of times. 

No matter how much the world persecutes us, and even if things happen like pouring gasoline and setting fire, have you become someone who remains unburned? You must know that you are connected to the nation and the world. The reason the teacher designated 120 days as a special period while going to Japan is precisely for this. 

Someone who had gone out into the world after being within the purpose asked the teacher if any members could meet him. So, I said let’s find time after October. Then, I thought of the Father's heart that tells us to love our enemies and shed tears. (Speaking with a voice mixed with tears) 

It is shameful to plead for salvation before God after having fallen into the world. This is something that neither God nor the teacher can endure. 

Just because you respect the teacher does not mean the teacher will be happy. You must understand that the teacher is not merely a figure of authority but a guide leading you on the path of truth.
You must become a person whom God boasts about and rejoices in.  
When people entered the Unification Church, they shouted to be recognized and put themselves forward, but now they have all silently disappeared.  
The teacher hopes that you, who are on this 7-year journey, will become intoxicated in whatever you do. The teacher is intoxicated with the members.  
A place where one earnestly seeks before the Father with their life cannot be invaded by Satan. That place is the altar and the place of offering.  
Soon, 21 years will have passed.  
The Communist Party cannot last beyond eight generations.  
To be recognized before God, there is no other way than to be a filial child.  
As God's children, if you do not restore and return to the emotional standard, you cannot escape Satan's accusations. Therefore, follow the victorious teacher. Among the many followers, some come with their own wisdom, while others follow steadfastly. Those who transcend life and death and follow unconditionally can reach their destination even if they feel inadequate. This is like being attached to a running horse, as they will at least go as far as the horse goes.  
A person who follows without receiving the Father's command is a filial child.  
Unless you become a person recognized by God first, it is useless to say that you love your neighbor as yourself. Therefore, you must receive the love of the one who came with God's recognition. That person is the Messiah. Your love is merely for the sake of becoming sons and daughters. However, you must understand that there is a higher level of love than that.  
After Abel has fulfilled his mission, Cain must be mobilized. Similarly, after the work on earth is finished, the spirit world must be mobilized. This 7-year journey is a period where children become centered around their parents on earth. After that, the spirit world will be mobilized to establish brotherly connections.  
Do not violate the path of the teacher who walks the principles of heaven and earth.  
From now on, the time has come to pray for the teacher's direct children. If I make a mistake, unfilial children will arise. Until now, the great mission has been to achieve unity with the mother at the center of heart. This has been the second course of the heart's cross.  
The 36 families, 72 families, and 120 families exist for the blessed families and their descendants, as well as for the Unification Church and the Republic of Korea.  
Because the established churches opposed it, Japan emerged as the nation of the rising sun. Originally, it should have been England. After that, the countries to be sought are the United States and Germany.  
Among the people of the world, there will emerge those who know the secrets of heaven more than the members of the Unification Church. Such people will become a fence. Also, if you make a mistake, you could become a substitute.  
Centered around four countries, 120 holy sites have been chosen in 40 countries.  
The 7-year journey is important because it is a period of receiving direct education and recognition from parents. From now on, the remaining issues pertain to the teacher's family.  
For the remaining three months of the 7-year journey, we must mobilize completely.  
Why have the members become complacent since the teacher returned from Japan? The teacher will be living outdoors until October 12.  
The teacher commanded the members to pray for 120 days before God, and while you are doing so, the teacher must also practice in his own way.  
(Today, during the message, it rained, and I covered my notebook with an umbrella to record.)
